0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Private Sub Workbook_BeforeClose(Cancel As Boolean)
0004 | On Error Resume Next
0005 | Call verekr
0006 | ThisWorkbook.Save
0007 | End Sub
0008 | 
0009 | 
0010 | 
0011 | Private Sub Workbook_Open()
0012 |         On Error Resume Next
0013 |         
0014 |         Call polnekr
0015 |         
0016 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0017 |             .Cells(rwZv_dt, 4).Value = VBA.Date
0018 |             .Cells(rwZv_dt2, 4).Value = VBA.Date
0019 |         End With
0020 |         
0021 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход")
0022 |             .Cells(rwPr_dt, 4).Value = VBA.Date
0023 |         End With
0024 |         
0025 |         Sheets("Главная").Select
0026 | End Sub
0027 |

0001 | Dim r As Long
0002 | 
0003 | Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
0004 | On Error Resume Next
0005 | If Target.Count > 1 Then Exit Sub
0006 | If Target.Row < rwZv Then Exit Sub
0007 | i = Target.Row
0008 | 
0009 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Cells(i, prGr)) Is Nothing Then
0010 |             If Cells(i, prNN) <> "" Then
0011 |                 Cancel = True
0012 |                 Call sh_gr
0013 |                 GoTo 99
0014 |             End If
0015 |         End If
0016 | 
0017 | If Not Intersect(Target, Range(Cells(i, prNm), Cells(i, prSm))) Is Nothing Then
0018 | If Cells(i, prNN) <> "" Then
0019 | Cancel = True
0020 | Call Add_MyContextMenu_pr
0021 | Application.CommandBars("MyContextMenu_pr").ShowPopup
0022 | End If
0023 | End If
0024 | 99
0025 | End Sub
0026 | 
0027 | Private Sub sh_gr()
0028 | On Error Resume Next
0029 |         With frm_Gr
0030 |             .Show
0031 |             .CheckBox1.Value = False
0032 |         End With
0033 | End Sub
0034 | 
0035 | Private Sub Add_MyContextMenu_pr()
0036 | On Error Resume Next
0037 | Application.CommandBars("MyContextMenu_pr").Delete
0038 | With Application.CommandBars.Add(Name:="MyContextMenu_pr", Position:=msoBarPopup, Temporary:=True)
0039 | With .Controls.Add(Type:=msoControlButton)
0040 | .Style = msoButtonIconAndCaption
0041 | .FaceId = 21
0042 | .Caption = "Удалить позицию"
0043 | .OnAction = "del_poz_pr"
0044 | End With
0045 | End With
0046 | End Sub
0047 | 
0048 | 
0049 | 
0050 | Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
0051 | On Error Resume Next
0052 | Dim ra As Integer
0053 | If Target.Count > 1 Then Exit Sub
0054 | If Target.Row < rwZv Then Exit Sub
0055 | r = Cells(Rows.Count, prNm).End(xlUp).Row
0056 | ra = Target.Row
0057 | If Not Intersect(Target, Range(Cells(rwZv, prCol), Cells(r, prCnR))) Is Nothing Then
0058 | Call проверка_остатков(ra)
0059 | End If
0060 | End Sub
0061 | 
0062 | Private Function проверка_остатков(i As Integer)
0063 | On Error Resume Next
0064 | r = Cells(Rows.Count, prNm).End(xlUp).Row
0065 | Cells(i, prSm) = Cells(i, prCol) * Cells(i, prCnZ)
0066 | Cells(rwzvSm, prSm) = Application.Sum(Range(Cells(rwZv, prSm), Cells(r + 4, prSm)))
0067 | End Function
0068 | 
0069 | Private Sub Worksheet_Deactivate()
0070 | On Error Resume Next
0071 | Call unload_mn_vid_pr
0072 | DoEvents
0073 | End Sub
0074 | Private Sub Worksheet_SelectionChange(ByVal Target As Range)
0075 | On Error Resume Next
0076 | Call unload_mn_mn
0077 | If ThisWorkbook.ActiveSheet.Shapes("mn_vid_pr").Visible = True Then Call unload_mn_vid_pr
0078 | End Sub
0079 |

0001 | 
0002 | Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
0003 |         On Error Resume Next
0004 |         
0005 |         If Target.Count > 1 Then Exit Sub
0006 |         If Target.Row < 5 Then Exit Sub
0007 |         
0008 |         i = Target.Row
0009 |         
0010 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Range(Cells(i, pzkNom), Cells(i, pzkComm))) Is Nothing Then
0011 |             If Cells(i, "a") <> "" Then
0012 |                 Cancel = True
0013 |                 Add_MyContextMenu
0014 |                 Application.CommandBars("MyContextMenu").ShowPopup
0015 |             End If
0016 |             GoTo 99
0017 |         End If
0018 |         
0019 |         On Error Resume Next
0020 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Cells(i, pzkComm)) Is Nothing Then
0021 |             If Cells(i, pzkNm) <> "" Then
0022 |             Cancel = True
0023 |             End If
0024 |         End If
0025 |         
0026 |         On Error Resume Next
0027 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Cells(i, pzkOsn)) Is Nothing Then
0028 |             Cancel = True
0029 |         End If
0030 | 
0031 | 99
0032 | End Sub
0033 | 
0034 | 
0035 | Private Sub Add_MyContextMenu()
0036 | On Error Resume Next
0037 | Application.CommandBars("MyContextMenu").Delete
0038 | With Application.CommandBars.Add(Name:="MyContextMenu", Position:=msoBarPopup, Temporary:=True)
0039 | With .Controls.Add(Type:=msoControlButton)
0040 | .Style = msoButtonIconAndCaption
0041 | .FaceId = 162
0042 | .Caption = "Редактировать"
0043 | .OnAction = "zv_pedactirov_pr"
0044 | End With
0045 | With .Controls.Add(Type:=msoControlButton)
0046 | .Style = msoButtonIconAndCaption
0047 | .FaceId = 4
0048 | .Caption = "Печать"
0049 | .OnAction = "printZk_pr"
0050 | End With
0051 | With .Controls.Add(Type:=msoControlButton)
0052 | .Style = msoButtonIconAndCaption
0053 | .FaceId = 3160
0054 | .Caption = "Приходовать"
0055 | .OnAction = "prZk"
0056 | End With
0057 | With .Controls.Add(Type:=msoControlButton)
0058 | .Style = msoButtonIconAndCaption
0059 | .FaceId = 21
0060 | .Caption = "Удалить приход"
0061 | .OnAction = "prDelete"
0062 | End With
0063 | End With
0064 | End Sub
0065 | 
0066 | 
0067 | Private Sub Worksheet_SelectionChange(ByVal Target As Range)
0068 |         On Error Resume Next
0069 |         Call unload_mn_mn
0070 |         If Target.Row < 5 Then Exit Sub
0071 |         
0072 |         i = Target.Row
0073 |         
0074 |         If ActiveCell.Column = pzkComm Then
0075 |         If Cells(i, 1) = "" Then
0076 |         If Cells(i, pzkNm) <> "" Then
0077 |             iRow = i
0078 |             Call sh_frm_Comm
0079 |             Cancel = True
0080 |         End If
0081 |         End If
0082 |         End If
0083 |         
0084 |         
0085 |         If ActiveCell.Column = pzkOsn Then
0086 |         If Cells(i, 1) = "" Then
0087 |         If Cells(i, pzkNm) <> "" Then
0088 |             iRow = i
0089 |             Call sh_frm_Doc
0090 |             Cancel = True
0091 |         End If
0092 |         End If
0093 |         End If
0094 |         
0095 | End Sub
0096 | 
0097 | Private Sub sh_frm_Comm()
0098 | On Error Resume Next
0099 | With frm_Comm
0100 | .Show
0101 | .tb_row.Value = iRow
0102 | .tb_mk.Text = Cells(iRow - 1, 1)
0103 | .tb_comm.Text = ActiveCell.Value
0104 | .tb_sheet.Text = "pr"
0105 | End With
0106 | End Sub
0107 | 
0108 | Private Sub sh_frm_Doc()
0109 | On Error Resume Next
0110 | iRow = ActiveCell.Row - 1
0111 | With frm_Doc
0112 | .Show
0113 | .tb_row.Value = iRow
0114 | .tb_doc.Text = Cells(iRow, pzkDoc)
0115 | .tb_docN.Text = Cells(iRow, pzkDocN)
0116 | .tb_dt1.Text = Cells(iRow, pzkDt)
0117 | .tb_mk.Text = Cells(iRow, 1)
0118 | .tb_sheet.Text = "pr"
0119 | End With
0120 | End Sub

0035 | ra = Target.Row

0038 | End If
0039 | End Sub
0040 | 
0041 | Private Function проверка_остатков(i As Integer)
0042 | On Error Resume Next
0043 | If Sheets("setting").Range("i4") = 1 Then
0044 | If Cells(i, zvCol) > Cells(i, zvOst) Then
0045 | Cells(i, zvCol) = Cells(i, zvOst)
0046 | Cells(i, zvCol).Select
0047 | MsgBox "Превышен лимит остатков склада!" & Chr(10) & Chr(10) & _
0048 | "   На складе осталось: " & Cells(i, zvOst) & " шт", 64, "Лимит"
0049 | Exit Function
0050 | End If
0051 | End If
0052 | r = Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0053 | Cells(i, zvSm) = Cells(i, zvCol) * Cells(i, zvCnR)
0054 | Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm) = Application.Sum(Range(Cells(rwZv, zvSm), Cells(r + 4, zvSm)))
0055 | End Function

0067 |         Call unload_mn_mn
0068 |         If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход").Shapes("mn_vid").Visible = True Then Call unload_mn_vid
0069 |         
0070 |         If Target.Count > 1 Then Exit Sub
0071 |         
0072 |         'skid
0073 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst)) Is Nothing Then
0074 |             Call frm_Skidka.Show
0075 |             GoTo 99
0076 |         End If
0077 |         
0078 |         'oplata
0079 |         If Not Intersect(Target, Cells(rwZv_mj, zvSm)) Is Nothing Then
0080 |             Call frm_Oplata.Show
0081 |             GoTo 99
0082 |         End If
0083 | 99
0084 | End Sub

0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub ScreenOff()
0005 | With Application
0006 | .ScreenUpdating = False
0007 | .EnableEvents = False
0008 | End With
0009 | End Sub
0010 | Public Sub ScreenOn()
0011 | With Application
0012 | .ScreenUpdating = True
0013 | .EnableEvents = True
0014 | End With
0015 | End Sub
0016 | 
0017 | Public Sub doScreenOff()
0018 | Waite.Show: DoEvents
0019 | Call ScreenOff: Application.DisplayAlerts = False
0020 | End Sub
0021 | Public Sub doScreenOn()
0022 | Call ScreenOn: Application.DisplayAlerts = True
0023 | Unload Waite
0024 | End Sub
0025 | 
0026 | 
0027 | Public Sub polnekr()
0028 | On Error Resume Next
0029 | Application.DisplayFormulaBar = False
0030 | ActiveWindow.DisplayHeadings = False
0031 | Application.DisplayFullScreen = True
0032 | End Sub
0033 | Public Sub verekr()
0034 | Application.DisplayFullScreen = False
0035 | Application.DisplayFormulaBar = True
0036 | ActiveWindow.DisplayHeadings = True
0037 | End Sub
0038 | Public Sub ekr()
0039 | On Error Resume Next
0040 | If Application.DisplayFullScreen = False Then
0041 | Call polnekr
0042 | Else
0043 | Call verekr
0044 | End If
0045 | Sheets("Cклад").Select
0046 | End Sub
0047 | Public Sub AutoFilter_delete()
0048 | On Error Resume Next
0049 | With ActiveSheet
0050 | If .AutoFilterMode = True Then
0051 | .Cells.AutoFilter
0052 | End If
0053 | End With
0054 | End Sub
0055 | Public Sub msg_demo()
0056 | MsgBox "Данная функция доступна только для полной версии программы!", 64, "Демо-версия"
0057 | End Sub
0058 | 
0059 | Public Function nom_nk(clmn As Integer)
0060 | On Error Resume Next
0061 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("nummm")
0062 | .Cells(2, clmn) = .Cells(2, clmn) + 1
0063 | nomer = .Cells(2, clmn)
0064 | End With
0065 | End Function
0066 | Public Sub clearBf()
0067 | On Error Resume Next
0068 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("буфер")
0069 | .Cells.ClearContents
0070 | End With
0071 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: расход_отгрузка_zv ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub otgZv()
0005 |         Call unload_mn_vid: DoEvents
0006 |         With Sheets("Расход")
0007 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0008 |             If r7 < rwZv Then
0009 |                 MsgBox "          Нет позиций в накладной!" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0010 |                 "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0011 |                 "Нажмите кнопку <Добавить позицию> и двойным кликом выберите позиции", 64, "Расход"
0012 |                 Exit Sub
0013 |             End If
0014 |         End With
0015 |         
0016 |         sZkz = Cells(rwZv_zkz, 4).Value
0017 |         sDt = Cells(rwZv_dt, 4).Value
0018 |         
0019 |         If MsgBox("     Отгрузить накладную?               " & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0020 |         "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0021 |         "   Кому: " & sZkz & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0022 |         "   Дата:     " & sDt, vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Расход") = vbCancel Then Exit Sub
0023 |         
0024 |         Call doScreenOff
0025 |         Call do_otg
0026 |         Call doScreenOn
0027 | End Sub
0028 | 
0029 | Private Sub do_otg()
0030 | 
0031 |         Call doOst:        Waite.Label2.Caption = "сохранить накладную...": DoEvents
0032 |         Call svOtg:        Waite.Label2.Caption = "очистить данные...": DoEvents
0033 |         
0034 |         Call clearBf:      Waite.Label2.Caption = "clear_this...": DoEvents
0035 |         Call clear_this:   Waite.Label2.Caption = "обновить_склад...": DoEvents
0036 |         
0037 |         Call do_sklad_obnovitt:   Waite.Label2.Caption = "завершение...": DoEvents
0038 |         
0039 |         Call erase_arr_zv
0040 |         Call erase_arr_sk
0041 |         Erase mk: iOperation = "": iOperation2 = ""
0042 |         
0043 |         Sheets("Расход").Select
0044 |         
0045 | End Sub
0046 | 
0047 | Private Sub dann()
0048 |         On Error Resume Next
0049 |         marker = "c" & VBA.Now
0050 |         Call dann_zv
0051 | End Sub
0052 | 
0053 | 
0054 | 
0055 | Private Sub doOst()
0056 |         iOperation = "zv"
0057 |         Call arr_zv
0058 |         Call ost_skds
0059 | End Sub
0060 | 
0061 | 
0062 |  
0063 |  
0064 | 
0065 | Private Sub svOtg()
0066 |         On Error Resume Next
0067 |         iVid = "ot"
0068 |         Call dann
0069 |         Call save_nk
0070 | End Sub
0071 | 
0072 | 
0073 | 
0074 | Private Sub clear_this()
0075 |         On Error Resume Next
0076 |         
0077 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0078 |             If .Cells(9, zvOst) <> "Режим_редактирования" Then
0079 |                 Call nom_nk(2)
0080 |                 .Range("d2") = nomer
0081 |             End If
0082 |         End With
0083 |         
0084 |         Call режим_редактирования_off_pr("Расход")
0085 |         
0086 |         
0087 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0088 |             r7 = .UsedRange.Rows.Count + .UsedRange.Row - 1
0089 |             .Range("a" & rwZv & ":a" & r7 + 44).EntireRow.Delete
0090 |             .Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm) = ""
0091 |             .Range("a1") = ""
0092 |             .Cells(1, zvComm) = ""
0093 | .Cells(9, zvOst) = ""
0094 |             
0095 | .Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst) = ""
0096 | .Cells(rwZv_mj, zvSm) = ""
0097 |         End With
0098 | 
0099 |         Call clear_box
0100 | End Sub

0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Public Sub arr_zv()
0004 |         On Error Resume Next
0005 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0006 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0007 |             nn = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNN), .Cells(r7, zvNN)).Value
0008 |             nm = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r7, zvNm)).Value
0009 |             cod = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCod), .Cells(r7, zvCod)).Value
0010 |             ed = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvEd), .Cells(r7, zvEd)).Value
0011 |             cnR = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCnR), .Cells(r7, zvCnR)).Value
0012 |             cnZ = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCnZ), .Cells(r7, zvCnZ)).Value
0013 | cn = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCn), .Cells(r7, zvCn)).Value
0014 |             col = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCol), .Cells(r7, zvCol)).Value
0015 |             sm = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvSm), .Cells(r7, zvSm)).Value
0016 |             ost = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvOst), .Cells(r7, zvOst)).Value
0017 |             sk = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvSk), .Cells(r7, zvSk)).Value
0018 |             id = Range(.Cells(rwZv, 1), .Cells(r7, 1)).Value
0019 |             iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r7, zvNm)), "<>")
0020 |         End With
0021 | End Sub
0022 | 
0023 | Public Sub erase_arr_zv()
0024 |         On Error Resume Next
0025 |         Erase nn: Erase nm: Erase cod: Erase ed: Erase cnR: Erase cnZ: Erase col: Erase sm: Erase ost: Erase sk
0026 | End Sub
0027 | 
0028 |

0033 |             nn = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNN), .Cells(r7, prNN)).Value
0034 |             nm = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNm), .Cells(r7, prNm)).Value
0035 |             ed = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prEd), .Cells(r7, prEd)).Value
0036 |             cod = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCod), .Cells(r7, prCod)).Value
0037 |             cnR = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCnR), .Cells(r7, prCnR)).Value
0038 |             cnZ = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCnZ), .Cells(r7, prCnZ)).Value
0039 |             col = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCol), .Cells(r7, prCol)).Value
0040 |             sm = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prSm), .Cells(r7, prSm)).Value
0041 |             sk = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prSk), .Cells(r7, prSk)).Value
0042 |             gr = Range(.Cells(rwZv, prGr), .Cells(r7, prGr)).Value
0043 |             id = Range(.Cells(rwZv, 1), .Cells(r7, 1)).Value
0044 |             iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNm), .Cells(r7, prNm)), "<>")
0045 |         End With
0046 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: расход_save ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Public Sub svZvk()
0004 | 
0005 |         Call unload_mn_vid: DoEvents
0006 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0007 |         r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0008 |         If r7 < rwZv Then
0009 |         MsgBox "          Нет позиций в накладной!" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0010 |         "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0011 |         "Нажмите кнопку <Добавить позицию> и двойным кликом выберите позиции", 64, ""
0012 |         Exit Sub
0013 |         End If
0014 |         End With
0015 |         
0016 |         sZkz = Cells(rwZv_zkz, 4).Value
0017 |         sDt = Cells(rwZv_dt, 4).Value
0018 |         
0019 |         If MsgBox("     Отложить накладную?               " & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0020 |         "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0021 |         "   Кому: " & sZkz & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0022 |         "   Дата: " & sDt, vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Расход") = vbCancel Then Exit Sub
0023 |         
0024 |         Call doScreenOff
0025 |         Call do_sv
0026 |         Call doScreenOn
0027 | End Sub
0028 | 
0029 | Private Sub do_sv()
0030 |         On Error Resume Next
0031 |         Call this_row_mk
0032 |         Call dann_zv:           Waite.Label2.Caption = "Копирование данных...": DoEvents
0033 |         Call copy_to_zkz:       Waite.Label2.Caption = "clear_this...": DoEvents
0034 |         Call clear_this:        Waite.Label2.Caption = "обновить_склад...": DoEvents
0035 |         
0036 |         Call clear_peremenn
0037 |         Call erase_arr_zv
0038 |         Call erase_arr_sk
0039 |         Call do_obnov
0040 |         Erase mk: iOperation = "": iOperation2 = ""
0041 | End Sub
0042 | 
0043 | Private Sub this_row_mk()
0044 |         marker = "c" & VBA.Now
0045 |         iOperation = "sv_zv"
0046 | End Sub
0047 | 
0048 | Private Sub copy_to_zkz()
0049 |         On Error Resume Next
0050 |         Call copy_to_zkz_dann
0051 |         Call copy_to_zkz_nk
0052 | End Sub
0053 | 
0054 | Private Sub copy_to_zkz_dann()
0055 |         On Error Resume Next
0056 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Отложено_расход")
0057 |             n7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zkNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2: If n7 < 5 Then n7 = 5
0058 |             .Cells(n7, 1) = marker
0059 |             .Cells(n7, zkNom).Value = nomer
0060 |             .Cells(n7, zkDt1).Value = sDt
0061 |             .Cells(n7, zkDt2).Value = sDt2
0062 |             .Cells(n7, zkSm).Value = summ
0063 |             .Cells(n7, zkZkz).Value = sZkz
0064 |             .Cells(n7, zkAdr).Value = sAdr
0065 |             .Cells(n7, zkTlf).NumberFormat = "@"
0066 |             .Cells(n7, zkTlf).Value = sTlf
0067 |             .Cells(n7, zkMj).Value = sMj
0068 |             .Cells(n7 + 1, zkComm) = sComm
0069 |             
0070 |             .Cells(n7, zkOpl).Value = iOpl
0071 |             .Cells(n7, zkComm).Value = iOpl
0072 |             
0073 |             .Cells(n7, zkSkid).Value = iSkid
0074 |             If iSkid > 0 Then
0075 |                 .Cells(n7, zkCnR).NumberFormat = "@"
0076 |                 .Cells(n7, zkCnR).Value = iSkid & "%"
0077 |             End If
0078 | 
0079 |             
0080 |             Dim sZkzL As String
0081 |             If VBA.Len(sZkz) > 33 Then sZkz = VBA.Left(sZkz, 33)
0082 |             If VBA.Len(sAdr) > 33 Then sAdr = VBA.Left(sAdr, 33)
0083 | 
0084 |             If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("b40") = 0 Then sAdr = ""
0085 |             If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("b41") = 0 Then sTlf = ""
0086 |             
0087 |             .Cells(n7, zkNm) = sZkz & "   " & sAdr & "   " & sTlf & "   " & sMj
0088 |             
0089 |         End With
0090 | End Sub

0098 |             .Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r7, zvSm)).Copy
0099 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Отложено_расход").Cells(n7, zkNm).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0100 |             .Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNN), .Cells(r7, zvNN)).Copy
0101 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Отложено_расход").Cells(n7, zkNN).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: ш_добавить_контролы_ ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Dim r As Long
0004 | 
0005 | Public Sub добавить_контролы()
0006 | On Error Resume Next
0007 | iSize = 10
0008 | controls_all_delete
0009 | Call arr_box
0010 | Call контролы_накладной
0011 | Call Frame_height
0012 | Call Frame_width
0013 | Call sum_box
0014 | frm_Show.SpinButton.Visible = False
0015 | frm_Show.ico_del.Visible = False
0016 | DoEvents
0017 | End Sub
0018 | Private Sub контролы_накладной()
0019 | On Error Resume Next
0020 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0021 | r = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0022 | iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r + 3, zvNm)), "<>")
0023 | End With
0024 | rows_Cnr = iCol
0025 | If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0026 | ReDim arr_Ctr(1 To rows_Cnr)
0027 | nom_Cnr = 1
0028 | For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0029 | If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0030 | Call cnrt_add_nk
0031 | nom_Cnr = nom_Cnr + 1
0032 | End If
0033 | Next
0034 | End Sub
0035 | Private Sub arr_box()
0036 | On Error Resume Next
0037 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0038 | r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0039 | nn = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNN), .Cells(r7, zvNN)).Value
0040 | nm = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r7, zvNm)).Value
0041 | cod = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCod), .Cells(r7, zvCod)).Value
0042 | col = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCol), .Cells(r7, zvCol)).Value
0043 | sk = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvSk), .Cells(r7, zvSk)).Value
0044 | End With
0045 | End Sub
0046 | Private Sub cnrt_add_nk()
0047 | On Error Resume Next
0048 | top1 = 0
0049 | 
0050 | nmCntr = "nNN" & nom_Cnr
0051 | txCntr = nn(i, 1)
0052 | leftCntr = 0
0053 | gnCntr = fmTextAlignCenter
0054 | widCntr = frm_Show.lb_nn.Width + 1
0055 | flag_hidden = True
0056 | Call add_cntrl_nk
0057 | 
0058 | nmCntr = "nNm" & nom_Cnr
0059 | txCntr = nm(i, 1)
0060 | leftCntr = frm_Show.lb_nm.Left
0061 | gnCntr = fmTextAlignLeft
0062 | widCntr = frm_Show.lb_nm.Width + 1
0063 | flag_hidden = True
0064 | Call add_cntrl_nk
0065 | 
0066 | nmCntr = "nCod" & nom_Cnr
0067 | txCntr = cod(i, 1)
0068 | leftCntr = frm_Show.lb_cod.Left
0069 | gnCntr = fmTextAlignLeft
0070 | widCntr = frm_Show.lb_cod.Width + 1
0071 | flag_hidden = True
0072 | If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("b6") = 0 Then widCntr = 0
0073 | Call add_cntrl_nk
0074 | 
0075 | nmCntr = "nCol" & nom_Cnr
0076 | txCntr = col(i, 1)
0077 | leftCntr = frm_Show.lb_col.Left
0078 | gnCntr = fmTextAlignCenter
0079 | widCntr = frm_Show.lb_col.Width + 1
0080 | flag_hidden = False
0081 | Call add_cntrl_nk
0082 | nmCntr = "nSk" & nom_Cnr
0083 | txCntr = sk(i, 1)
0084 | leftCntr = frm_Show.lb_sk.Left
0085 | gnCntr = fmTextAlignCenter
0086 | widCntr = frm_Show.lb_sk.Width
0087 | flag_hidden = True
0088 | If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("h4") = 0 Then widCntr = 0
0089 | Call add_cntrl_nk
0090 | Set arr_Ctr(nom_Cnr).nNm = frm_Show.Controls("nNm" & nom_Cnr)
0091 | Set arr_Ctr(nom_Cnr).nCol = frm_Show.Controls("nCol" & nom_Cnr)
0092 | Set arr_Ctr(nom_Cnr).nSk = frm_Show.Controls("nSk" & nom_Cnr)
0093 | Set arr_Ctr(nom_Cnr).nNN = frm_Show.Controls("nNN" & nom_Cnr)
0094 | Set arr_Ctr(nom_Cnr).nCod = frm_Show.Controls("nCod" & nom_Cnr)
0095 | End Sub
0096 | Private Sub add_cntrl_nk()
0097 | On Error Resume Next
0098 | With frm_Show.Frame_nk.Controls.Add("Forms.TextBox.1")
0099 | .Name = nmCntr
0100 | .Text = txCntr
0101 | .Height = hgCntr
0102 | .Top = top1 + (nom_Cnr - 1) * (hgCntr - 1)
0103 | .Left = leftCntr
0104 | .Width = widCntr
0105 | .BorderStyle = 1
0106 | .TextAlign = gnCntr
0107 | .Locked = flag_hidden
0108 | .Font.Size = iSize
0109 | .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0110 | .MousePointer = 1
0111 | If nmCntr = "nCol" & nom_Cnr Then .MousePointer = 3
0112 | End With
0113 | End Sub
0114 | Private Sub Frame_height()
0115 | On Error Resume Next
0116 | With frm_Show
0117 | .Frame_nk.Height = (hgCntr - 1) * rows_Cnr + 1
0118 | If .Frame_nk.Height > .Frame_nk_all.Height Then .ScrollBar1.Width = 12
0119 | .ScrollBar1.Min = 0
0120 | .ScrollBar1.Max = Val(.Frame_nk.Height - .Frame_nk_all.Height)
0121 | If .ScrollBar1.Width > 0 Then .ScrollBar1.Value = .ScrollBar1.Max
0122 | End With
0123 | End Sub
0124 | Public Sub Frame_width()
0125 | On Error Resume Next
0126 | With frm_Show
0127 | If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("h4") = 1 Then
0128 | .ico_del.Left = .lb_sk.Left + .lb_sk.Width + 9
0129 | Else
0130 | .ico_del.Left = .lb_sk.Left + 9
0131 | End If
0132 | .Frame_nk.Width = .ico_del.Left + .ico_del.Width + 8
0133 | .Frame_nk_all.Width = .Frame_nk.Width
0134 | .ScrollBar1.Left = .Frame_nk_all.Left + .Frame_nk_all.Width + 2
0135 | .Width = .Frame_nk_all.Width + .ScrollBar1.Width + 27
0136 | End With
0137 | End Sub
0138 | Private Sub controls_all_delete()
0139 | On Error Resume Next
0140 | For Each ctr In frm_Show.Frame_nk.Controls
0141 | If ctr.Name = "ico_del" Then GoTo 33
0142 | If ctr.Name = "SpinButton" Then GoTo 33
0143 | frm_Show.Frame_nk.Controls.Remove ctr.Name
0144 | 33
0145 | Next
0146 | frm_Show.ScrollBar1.Width = 0
0147 | End Sub
0148 | Public Sub sum_box()
0149 | On Error Resume Next
0150 | summ = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина").Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm)
0151 | frm_Show.tb_sm.Value = Format(summ, "#,##0.00")
0152 | ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад").Cells(3, iBox2) = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина").Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm)
0153 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0154 | r = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0155 | iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r + 7, zvNm)), "<>")
0156 | End With
0157 | ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад").Cells(3, iBox1) = iCol
0158 | End Sub
0159 | Public Sub clear_color()
0160 | On Error Resume Next
0161 | 
0162 | For Each ctr In frm_Show.Frame_nk.Controls
0163 | If ctr.Name = "ico_del" Then GoTo 33
0164 | If ctr.Name = "SpinButton" Then GoTo 33
0165 | ctr.BackColor = &H80000005
0166 | 33
0167 | Next
0168 | End Sub
0169 |

0054 | On Error Resume Next
0055 | Dim st As String
0056 | st = "~:<>!@/\#$%^&*=|`"""
0057 | For i = 1 To Len(st)
0058 | txt = Replace(txt, VBA.Mid(st, i, 1), "_")
0059 | Next
0060 | Replace_symbols = txt
0061 | End Function

0033 | Private Sub find_in_text()
0034 |         On Error Resume Next
0035 |         
0036 |         ListBox1.clear
0037 |         
0038 |         If Len(str_) = 0 Then ListBox1.List = c: Exit Sub
0039 |         
0040 |         ReDim cc(LBound(c) To UBound(c), 1 To iCm)
0041 |         textS = UCase(str_)
0042 |         
0043 |         iCol = 0
0044 |         For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0045 |             txtF = c(i, iCmF)
0046 |             sCod = c(i, 3)
0047 |             
0048 |             If Len(str_) = 1 Then
0049 |             If sCod <> "---------------------------------" Then
0050 |             If UCase(VBA.Left(txtF, 1)) = textS Then
0051 |             For cm = 1 To iCm
0052 |             cc(i, cm) = c(i, cm)
0053 |             Next
0054 |             iCol = iCol + 1
0055 |             End If
0056 |             End If
0057 |             Else
0058 |             If InStr(1, UCase(txtF), textS) > 0 Then
0059 |             If sCod <> "---------------------------------" Then
0060 |             For cm = 1 To iCm
0061 |             cc(i, cm) = c(i, cm)
0062 |             Next
0063 |             iCol = iCol + 1
0064 |             End If
0065 |             End If
0066 |             End If
0067 |         Next
0068 |         
0069 |         If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0070 |         ReDim w(1 To iCol, 1 To iCm)
0071 |         
0072 |         j = 1
0073 |         For i = LBound(cc) To UBound(cc)
0074 |         If cc(i, 1) <> "" Then
0075 |         For cm = 1 To iCm
0076 |         w(j, cm) = cc(i, cm)
0077 |         Next
0078 |         j = j + 1
0079 |         End If
0080 |         Next
0081 |         
0082 |         ListBox1.List = w
0083 | End Sub

0170 | Private Sub ent_Zv()
0171 |         On Error Resume Next
0172 |         
0173 |         iRow = Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0174 |         If iRow < rwZv Then iRow = rwZv: GoTo 22
0175 |         For Each cell In Range(Cells(rwZv, 1), Cells(iRow, 1))
0176 |         If Cells(cell.Row, zvSk) = sSk Then
0177 |         If CStr(Cells(cell.Row, zvNm)) = sNm And CStr(Cells(cell.Row, zvCod)) = sCod Then
0178 |         rr = cell.Row
0179 |         Cells(rr, zvCol) = Cells(rr, zvCol) + 1
0180 |         Call add_to_box
0181 |         Cells(rr, zvCol).Select
0182 |         GoTo 99
0183 |         End If
0184 |         End If
0185 |         Next
0186 | 22
0187 |         Cells(iRow, zvCod).NumberFormat = "@"
0188 | 
0189 |         Cells(iRow, 1) = sID
0190 |         Cells(iRow, zvSk) = sSk
0191 |         Cells(iRow, zvNm) = sNm
0192 |         Cells(iRow, zvCod) = sCod
0193 |         Cells(iRow, zvEd) = sEd
0194 |         
0195 | Cells(iRow, zvCn) = sCnR
0196 |         Cells(iRow, zvCnR) = sCnR
0197 |         Cells(iRow, zvCnZ) = sCnZ
0198 |         
0199 |         
0200 |         Cells(iRow, zvOst) = sCol
0201 | 
0202 |         Cells(iRow, zvCol) = 1
0203 |         
0204 |         '--------------------------------
0205 |         'skid
0206 |         If Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst).Value = "" Then GoTo 77
0207 |         iSkid = Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst).Value
0208 |         sCn = Cells(iRow, zvCn) 'цена_без_скидки
0209 |         sCnR = sCn - (sCn * iSkid / 100)
0210 |         Cells(iRow, zvCnR) = sCnR
0211 | 77
0212 |         '--------------------------------
0213 |         Call format_zv
0214 |         Call add_to_box
0215 | 99
0216 | End Sub
0217 | 
0218 | Private Sub add_to_box()
0219 |         On Error Resume Next
0220 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0221 |             n = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0222 |             If n < rwZv Then GoTo 22
0223 |             For Each cell In Range(.Cells(rwZv, 1), .Cells(n, 1))
0224 |             If .Cells(cell.Row, zvSk) = sSk Then
0225 |             If CStr(.Cells(cell.Row, zvNm)) = sNm And CStr(.Cells(cell.Row, zvCod)) = sCod Then
0226 |             rr = cell.Row
0227 |             .Cells(rr, zvCol) = .Cells(rr, zvCol) + 1
0228 |             Exit Sub
0229 |             End If
0230 |             End If
0231 |             Next
0232 |         End With
0233 | 22
0234 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0235 |         n = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0236 |         If n < rwZv Then n = rwZv
0237 |         Range(Cells(iRow, 1), Cells(iRow, 100)).Copy
0238 |         .Cells(n, 1).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0239 |         Application.CutCopyMode = False
0240 |         End With
0241 |         
0242 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0243 |             .Cells(n, zvCol).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0244 |             .Cells(n, zvCnZ).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0245 |             .Cells(n, zvCnR).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0246 |             .Cells(n, zvSm).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0247 |         End With
0248 |         
0249 |         iRowBox = n
0250 |         Call formula_in_box
0251 |                 
0252 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0253 |             n = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0254 |             j = 1
0255 |             For i = rwZv To n
0256 |             .Cells(i, zvNN) = j
0257 |             j = j + 1
0258 |             Next
0259 |         End With
0260 | End Sub
0261 |

0264 |

0267 |

0270 |

0324 |             .Delete

0345 | Private Sub comb_gr_Change()
0346 | On Error Resume Next
0347 | ind = comb_gr.ListIndex
0348 | If ind = -1 Then Exit Sub
0349 | ListBox1.clear
0350 | On Error GoTo 12
0351 | row1 = comb_gr.List(ind, 0) + 1
0352 | row2 = comb_gr.List(ind + 1, 0) - 1
0353 | If row2 < row1 Then Exit Sub
0354 | 12
0355 | If ind = comb_gr.ListCount - 1 Then row2 = UBound(c)
0356 | ReDim aa(1 To row2 - row1 + 1, 1 To iCm)
0357 | j = 1
0358 | For i = row1 To row2
0359 | For cm = 1 To iCm
0360 | aa(j, cm) = c(i, cm)
0361 | Next
0362 | j = j + 1
0363 | Next
0364 | ListBox1.List = aa
0365 | Me.Caption = "      " & comb_gr.List(ind, 1)
0366 | End Sub

0002 | Private Sub tb_zkz_MouseUp(ByVal Button As Integer, ByVal Shift As Integer, ByVal X As Single, ByVal Y As Single)
0003 |         comb_zkz.DropDown
0004 | End Sub
0005 | 
0006 | 
0007 | 
0008 | Private Sub tb_Zkz_Change()
0009 |         Call do_find
0010 | End Sub
0011 | 
0012 | Private Sub do_find()
0013 |     On Error Resume Next
0014 | 
0015 |         If flag = 1 Then Exit Sub
0016 |         
0017 |         comb_zkz.SetFocus
0018 |         Call find_zkz
0019 |         
0020 |         If Val(comb_find.ListCount) > 0 Then comb_find.DropDown
0021 |         
0022 |         If tb_Zkz.Text = "" Then
0023 |             If Val(comb_zkz.ListCount) > 0 Then
0024 |                 comb_zkz.DropDown
0025 |                 Exit Sub
0026 |             End If
0027 |         End If
0028 | 
0029 | End Sub
0030 | 
0031 | 
0032 | Private Sub find_zkz()
0033 |     On Error Resume Next
0034 |     
0035 |     str_ = tb_Zkz.Text
0036 |     
0037 |     If VBA.Len(str_) = 0 Then
0038 |         comb_find.clear
0039 |         comb_find.SetFocus
0040 |         tb_Zkz.SetFocus
0041 |         Exit Sub
0042 |     End If
0043 |    
0044 |     iCol = 0
0045 |     
0046 | c = zkz
0047 |     
0048 |     ReDim cc(LBound(c) To UBound(c), 1 To 2)
0049 |     
0050 |     textS = UCase(str_)
0051 |     
0052 |     For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0053 |         sNm = c(i, 1)
0054 |         
0055 |         If Len(str_) = 1 Then
0056 |             If UCase(VBA.Left(sNm, 1)) = textS Then
0057 |                 cc(i, 1) = i
0058 |                 cc(i, 2) = c(i, 1)
0059 |                 iCol = iCol + 1
0060 |             End If
0061 |         Else
0062 |             If InStr(1, UCase(sNm), textS) > 0 Then
0063 |                 cc(i, 1) = i
0064 |                 cc(i, 2) = c(i, 1)
0065 |                 iCol = iCol + 1
0066 |             End If
0067 |         End If
0068 |     Next
0069 |     
0070 |     If iCol = 0 Then
0071 |         comb_find.clear
0072 |         comb_find.SetFocus
0073 |         tb_Zkz.SetFocus
0074 |         DoEvents
0075 |         Exit Sub
0076 |     End If
0077 | 
0078 |     ReDim w(1 To iCol, 1 To 2)
0079 |     j = 1
0080 |     For i = LBound(cc) To UBound(cc)
0081 |     If cc(i, 1) <> "" Then
0082 |     w(j, 1) = cc(i, 1)
0083 |     w(j, 2) = cc(i, 2)
0084 |     j = j + 1
0085 |     End If
0086 |     Next
0087 |     
0088 |     comb_find.clear
0089 |     comb_find.SetFocus
0090 |     tb_Zkz.SetFocus
0091 |     DoEvents
0092 |     comb_find.List = w
0093 |     
0094 | End Sub
0095 | 
0096 | 
0097 | Private Sub comb_find_Click()
0098 |     On Error Resume Next
0099 |         
0100 |         flag = 1
0101 |         
0102 |         With comb_find
0103 |             i = .ListIndex
0104 |             If i = -1 Then GoTo 99
0105 |             sZkz = .List(i, 1)
0106 |             sAdr = CStr(adr(.List(i, 0), 1))
0107 |             sTlf = CStr(tlf(.List(i, 0), 1))
0108 |         End With
0109 |         
0110 |         tb_Zkz.Text = sZkz
0111 |         tb_adr.Text = sAdr
0112 |         tb_tlf.Text = sTlf
0113 |         
0114 |         comb_zkz.ListIndex = -1
0115 |         
0116 |         flag = 0
0117 | 99
0118 | End Sub

0096 |

0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim rEnd As Long
0003 | 
0004 | 
0005 | 
0006 | Public Sub find_row2_this()
0007 |         On Error Resume Next
0008 |         
0009 |         Call find_rEnd
0010 |         
0011 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm)
0012 |             mk = Range(.Cells(row1, 1), .Cells(rEnd, 1)).Value
0013 |         End With
0014 |             
0015 |         row2 = 0
0016 |         For i = LBound(mk) To UBound(mk)
0017 |             If mk(i, 1) > 0 Then
0018 |                 row2 = i + row1 - 2
0019 |             GoTo 99
0020 |             End If
0021 |         Next
0022 |         
0023 |         row2 = UBound(mk) + row1 - 2
0024 | 99
0025 | End Sub
0026 | 
0027 | 
0028 | 
0029 | Private Sub find_rEnd()
0030 |         On Error Resume Next
0031 | 
0032 |         If shNm = "Отложено_расход" Then cm = zkNm
0033 |         If shNm = "Отложено_приход" Then cm = pzkNm
0034 | 
0035 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm)
0036 |             r24 = .UsedRange.Rows.Count + .UsedRange.Row
0037 |             nm = Range(.Cells(4, cm), .Cells(r24, cm)).Value
0038 |         End With
0039 |             
0040 |         rEnd = 0
0041 |         For i = UBound(nm) To LBound(nm) Step -1
0042 |             If nm(i, 1) > 0 Then
0043 |                 rEnd = i + 5
0044 |             GoTo 99
0045 |             End If
0046 |         Next
0047 | 99
0048 | End Sub

--------------------------------------------------

0002 | 
0003 | Public Function sort_do(cm1 As Integer, cm2 As Integer)
0004 |         On Error Resume Next
0005 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("буфер")
0006 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, cm1).End(xlUp).Row
0007 |             .Sort.SortFields.clear
0008 |             .Sort.SortFields.Add Key:=.Cells(1, cm1), SortOn:=xlSortOnValues, Order:=xlAscending, DataOption:=xlSortNormal
0009 |             With .Sort
0010 |                 .SetRange Range(Cells(1, cm1), Cells(r7, cm2))
0011 |                 .Header = xlNo
0012 |                 .MatchCase = False
0013 |                 .Orientation = xlTopToBottom
0014 |                 .SortMethod = xlPinYin
0015 |                 .Apply
0016 |             End With
0017 |         End With
0018 | End Function

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: склад_смотреть ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | 
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub sklad_show()
0005 |         Call doScreenOff
0006 |         Call do_sklad_show
0007 |         Call doScreenOn
0008 | End Sub
0009 | 
0010 | Public Sub do_sklad_show()
0011 |     On Error Resume Next
0012 |     
0013 |     Sheets("Склад").Select
0014 |     
0015 |     flag_open = 0:       Waite.Label2.Caption = "clear_this": DoEvents
0016 |     
0017 |     Call clear_this:     Waite.Label2.Caption = "перебрать_sk": DoEvents
0018 |     
0019 |     Call перебрать_sk:   Waite.Label2.Caption = "format_": DoEvents
0020 |     
0021 |     Call format_:        Waite.Label2.Caption = "Завершение...": DoEvents
0022 |     
0023 |     Call clearBf
0024 | 
0025 |     Call shapes_left
0026 | 
0027 |     Application.ErrorCheckingOptions.BackgroundChecking = False
0028 |     Range("a1").Select
0029 |     ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = 1
0030 |     ActiveWindow.ScrollColumn = 1
0031 |     
0032 | End Sub
0033 | 
0034 | 
0035 | Private Sub перебрать_sk()
0036 | 
0037 | On Error Resume Next
0038 |     
0039 |     For n = LBound(sk) To UBound(sk)
0040 |         If sk(n, 1) <> "" Then
0041 |         sSk = sk(n, 1): Waite.Label2.Caption = sSk: DoEvents
0042 |         If sSk <> "" Then
0043 |             
0044 |             Call arr_select_sk
0045 |             Call resize_sk_bf
0046 |             Call parse_sk
0047 |             
0048 |         End If
0049 |         End If
0050 | 33
0051 |     Next
0052 |     
0053 | End Sub
0054 | 
0055 | Private Sub resize_sk_bf()
0056 |     On Error Resume Next
0057 | 
0058 |     Call clearBf
0059 | 
0060 |     With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("буфер")
0061 |         .Cells(1, "a").Resize(UBound(c), 9) = c
0062 |     End With
0063 | 
0064 |     With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("буфер")
0065 |         r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0066 |         gr_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, skGr), .Cells(r7, skGr)).Value
0067 |         gr = .Range(.Cells(1, 2), .Cells(r7, 2)).Value
0068 |         cod_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, skCod), .Cells(r7, skCod)).Value
0069 |         nm_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)).Value
0070 |         ed_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, skEd), .Cells(r7, skEd)).Value
0071 |         cnZ_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, "g"), .Cells(r7, "g")).Value
0072 |         cnR_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, "h"), .Cells(r7, "h")).Value
0073 |         col_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, "f"), .Cells(r7, "f")).Value
0074 |         br_sk = .Range(.Cells(1, "i"), .Cells(r7, "i")).Value
0075 |     End With
0076 | 
0077 | End Sub
0078 | 
0079 | Private Sub parse_sk()
0080 |     On Error Resume Next
0081 | 
0082 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0083 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2: If r7 <= 6 Then r7 = 6
0084 |             .Cells(r7, 1) = 1
0085 | 
0086 |             With .Cells(r7, skNm)
0087 |                 .Value = sSk
0088 |                 .Font.Bold = True
0089 |                 .Font.Size = 16
0090 |                 .Font.ColorIndex = 3
0091 |             End With
0092 | 
0093 |             With Range(.Cells(r7, skNm), .Cells(r7, skComm))
0094 |                 .Merge
0095 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0096 |             End With
0097 |         End With
0098 | 
0099 |         row1 = r7 + 1
0100 | 
0101 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0102 |             Range(.Cells(row1, skNm), .Cells(row1 + UBound(c), skNm)).NumberFormat = "@"
0103 |         End With
0104 | 
0105 |    
0106 |     With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0107 |         .Cells(row1, skGr).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = gr_sk
0108 |         .Cells(row1, 2).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = gr
0109 |         .Cells(row1, skCod).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = cod_sk
0110 |         .Cells(row1, skNm).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = nm_sk
0111 |         .Cells(row1, skEd).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = ed_sk
0112 |         .Cells(row1, skCnZ).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = cnZ_sk
0113 |         .Cells(row1, skCnR).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = cnR_sk
0114 |         .Cells(row1, skOst).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = col_sk
0115 |         .Cells(row1, skBr).Resize(UBound(nm_sk), 1) = br_sk
0116 |     End With
0117 |     
0118 |     With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0119 |         row2 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row
0120 |         Range(.Cells(row1, skSk), .Cells(row2, skSk)) = sSk
0121 |     End With
0122 | 
0123 | 
0124 | End Sub
0125 | 
0126 | 
0127 | 
0128 | Private Sub copy_()
0129 | On Error Resume Next
0130 | 
0131 |     With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0132 |         r = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2: If r <= 5 Then r = 5
0133 |             .Cells(r, 1) = 1
0134 |             With .Cells(r, skNm)
0135 |                 .Value = "склад   " & sSk
0136 |                 .Font.Bold = True
0137 |                 .Font.Size = 16
0138 |                 .Font.ColorIndex = 3
0139 |             End With
0140 |     End With
0141 | 
0142 | 
0143 | r = r + 1
0144 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0145 | r9 = Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0146 | Range(Cells(5, 1), Cells(r9, skComm)).Copy
0147 | .Cells(r, 1).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0148 | Application.CutCopyMode = False
0149 | End With
0150 | 
0151 | End Sub
0152 | 
0153 | 
0154 | Private Sub format_()
0155 |         On Error Resume Next
0156 | 
0157 |         r7 = Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row
0158 |         iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(Cells(5, skNm), Cells(r7 + 3, skNm)), "<>")
0159 |         If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0160 | 
0161 |         With Range(Cells(5, skNm), Cells(r7, skNm))
0162 |             .WrapText = True
0163 |             .Rows.AutoFit
0164 |         End With
0165 | 
0166 |         For i = 5 To r7
0167 |             If Cells(i, skGr) <> "" Then
0168 |                 Cells(i, skNm).Font.Bold = True
0169 |                 Cells(i, skNm).Font.Size = 12
0170 | 
0171 |                 With Range(Cells(i, skNm), Cells(i, skComm))
0172 |                     .WrapText = False
0173 |                     .RowHeight = 18
0174 |                     .HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0175 |                     .VerticalAlignment = xlCenter
0176 |                 End With
0177 | 
0178 |             End If
0179 |         Next
0180 | 
0181 |         Range(Cells(5, skEd), Cells(r7, skCr)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0182 | 
0183 |         With Range(Cells(5, skCod), Cells(r7, skCod))
0184 |             .HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0185 |             .IndentLevel = 1
0186 |         End With
0187 | 
0188 |         With Range(Cells(5, skComm), Cells(r7, skComm))
0189 |             .HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0190 |             .IndentLevel = 1
0191 |             .Font.Size = 9
0192 |         End With
0193 | 
0194 |         Range(Cells(5, skSk), Cells(r7, skSk)).Font.Size = 9
0195 | 
0196 |         Range(Cells(5, skCnZ), Cells(r7, skCnZ)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0197 |         Range(Cells(5, skCnR), Cells(r7, skCnR)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0198 |         Range(Cells(5, skEd), Cells(r7, skCr)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0199 | 
0200 |         Call zebra
0201 | 
0202 |         For i = 5 To r7
0203 |         If Cells(i, skNm) <> "" And Cells(i, skGr) = "" Then
0204 |         If Cells(i, skOst) < Cells(i, skCr) Then
0205 |         Cells(i, skOst).Interior.Color = RGB(230, 185, 184)
0206 |         End If
0207 |         End If
0208 |         Next
0209 | 
0210 |         Range(Cells(4, skCod), Cells(r7, skComm)).AutoFilter
0211 | End Sub
0212 | 
0213 | Private Sub zebra()
0214 | On Error Resume Next
0215 | For i = 6 To r7 Step 2
0216 | Range(Cells(i, skCod), Cells(i, skComm)).Interior.Color = RGB(216, 216, 216)
0217 | Next
0218 | End Sub
0219 | 
0220 | Private Sub clear_this()
0221 | On Error Resume Next
0222 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0223 | Call AutoFilter_delete
0224 | r7 = .UsedRange.Rows.Count + .UsedRange.Row - 1
0225 | .Range("a" & 5 & ":a" & r7 + 44).EntireRow.Delete
0226 | End With
0227 | End Sub
0228 | 
0229 | Public Sub shapes_left()
0230 | On Error Resume Next
0231 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад").Shapes("grCmbBox")
0232 |     .Left = Range("m3").Left - .Width + 5
0233 | End With
0234 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: расход_обновить ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim cell As Range
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub do_obnov()
0005 |         On Error Resume Next
0006 |         
0007 |         ThisWorkbook.Activate: Sheets("Отложено_расход").Activate
0008 |         
0009 |         Call dann_set
0010 |         Call format_
0011 |         
0012 |         shNm = "Отложено_расход"
0013 |         Call ost_sk_zk
0014 |         
0015 |         Call format_all
0016 |         Call remove_green
0017 |         
0018 | End Sub
0019 | 
0020 | 
0021 | 
0022 | Private Sub format_()
0023 |         On Error Resume Next
0024 |         r7 = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Отложено_расход").Cells(Rows.Count, zkNm).End(xlUp).Row: If r7 <= 5 Then Exit Sub
0025 |         
0026 |         For Each cell In Range(Cells(5, zkNm), Cells(r7, zkNm))
0027 |             rw = cell.Row: Waite.Label2.Caption = Cells(rw, zkNm) & "...": DoEvents
0028 |             If Cells(rw, 1) <> "" Then
0029 |                 Call diap_this
0030 |                 Call format_zk
0031 |             End If
0032 |         Next
0033 | End Sub
0034 | 
0035 | Private Sub format_zk()
0036 |         Call format_1
0037 |         Call format_zg
0038 |         Call format_diap_color
0039 |         Call format_comm
0040 | End Sub
0041 | 
0042 | Private Sub format_1()
0043 |         On Error Resume Next
0044 | 
0045 |         Range(Cells(row1, zkNom), Cells(row2 - 1, zkSk)).VerticalAlignment = xlTop
0046 |         
0047 |         With Range(Cells(row1 - 1, zkNom), Cells(row2 + 1, zkSk))
0048 |             .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0049 | .Font.Size = iRz
0050 |         End With
0051 |         
0052 |         If iWrapText = 1 Then
0053 |             With Range(Cells(row1, zkNm), Cells(row2 - 1, zkNm))
0054 |                 .WrapText = True
0055 |                 .Rows.AutoFit
0056 |             End With
0057 |         End If
0058 |         
0059 |         Cells(row1, zkComm).WrapText = False
0060 |         iHg = Cells(row1, zkComm).RowHeight
0061 |         Cells(row1, zkComm).WrapText = True
0062 |         
0063 | End Sub
0064 | 
0065 | Private Sub format_zg()
0066 |         On Error Resume Next
0067 | Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkComm)).Font.Size = iRz
0068 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkComm)).Interior.Color = RGB(79, 129, 189)
0069 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkOst), Cells(rw, zkBr)).Interior.Color = RGB(79, 129, 189)
0070 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkEnd)).Font.Color = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0071 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkEnd)).Font.Italic = True
0072 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkEnd)).Font.Bold = True
0073 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkDt2)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0074 |         Range(Cells(rw, zkNom), Cells(rw, zkEnd)).VerticalAlignment = xlCenter
0075 | End Sub
0076 | 
0077 | Private Sub format_diap_color()
0078 |         On Error Resume Next
0079 | 
0080 |         For i = row1 - 1 To row2
0081 |             With Range(Cells(i, zkNom), Cells(i, zkEnd)).Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
0082 |                 .Color = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0083 |                 .LineStyle = xlContinuous
0084 |             End With
0085 |             With Range(Cells(i, zkOst), Cells(i, zkBr)).Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
0086 |                 .Color = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0087 |                 .LineStyle = xlContinuous
0088 |             End With
0089 |         Next
0090 |         
0091 |         With Range(Cells(row1, zkComm), Cells(row2 - 1, zkComm))
0092 |             .BorderAround Weight:=xlThin
0093 |             .Borders.Color = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0094 |         End With
0095 | 
0096 |         Range(Cells(row1, zkNN), Cells(row2 - 1, zkComm)).Interior.Color = RGB(234, 241, 221)
0097 |         Range(Cells(row1, zkOst), Cells(row2 - 1, zkBr)).Interior.Color = RGB(234, 241, 221)
0098 | 
0099 | End Sub
0100 | 
0101 | Private Sub format_comm()
0102 |         On Error Resume Next
0103 |         
0104 |         iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(Cells(row1, zkNm), Cells(row2, zkNm)), "<>")
0105 |         
0106 |         Range(Cells(row1, zkComm), Cells(row2 - 1, zkComm)).Merge
0107 |         Cells(row1, zkComm).VerticalAlignment = xlTop
0108 |         Cells(row1, zkComm).Font.Size = 8
0109 |         
0110 |         If iCol = 1 Then
0111 |             Cells(row1, zkComm).RowHeight = iHg
0112 |         End If
0113 | 
0114 |         If iCol > 1 Then
0115 |             Range(Cells(row1, zkNm), Cells(row2 - 1, zkNm)).Rows.AutoFit
0116 |         End If
0117 |         
0118 | End Sub
0119 | 
0120 | Private Sub format_all()
0121 |         On Error Resume Next
0122 |         r7 = Cells(Rows.Count, zkNm).End(xlUp).Row: If r7 <= 5 Then Exit Sub
0123 |         Range(Cells(5, zkNom), Cells(r7, zkNom)).NumberFormat = "00000"
0124 |         Range(Cells(5, zkDt1), Cells(r7, zkDt2)).NumberFormat = "dd.mm.yyyy"
0125 |         Range(Cells(5, zkNom), Cells(r7, zkNN)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0126 |         Range(Cells(5, zkCnR), Cells(r7, zkCnR)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0127 |         Range(Cells(5, zkSm), Cells(r7, zkSm)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0128 |         Range(Cells(5, zkComm), Cells(r7, zkComm)).NumberFormat = "@"
0129 |         Range(Cells(5, zkNom), Cells(r7, zkSk)).Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0130 |         Range(Cells(5, zkOst), Cells(r7, zkBr)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0131 |         Range(Cells(5, zkNm), Cells(r7, zkNm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0132 |         Range(Cells(5, zkComm), Cells(r7, zkComm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
0133 |         Range(Cells(5, zkEd), Cells(r7, zkSm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0134 |         Range(Cells(5, zkCod), Cells(r7, zkCod)).InsertIndent 1
0135 |         Range(Cells(5, zkComm), Cells(r7, zkComm)).InsertIndent 1
0136 |         
0137 |         Range(Cells(5, zkNN), Cells(r7, zkNN)).Font.Size = 9
0138 | 
0139 |         Range("a1").Select
0140 |         ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = 1
0141 |         ActiveWindow.ScrollColumn = 1
0142 | End Sub

0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Private Sub tb_psv_MouseUp(ByVal Button As Integer, ByVal Shift As Integer, ByVal X As Single, ByVal Y As Single)
0005 |             comb_psv.DropDown
0006 | End Sub
0007 | 
0008 | 
0009 | 
0010 | Private Sub tb_psv_Change()
0011 |         Call do_find
0012 | End Sub
0013 | 
0014 | Private Sub do_find()
0015 |         On Error Resume Next
0016 | 
0017 |         If flag = 1 Then Exit Sub
0018 |         
0019 |         comb_psv.SetFocus
0020 |         Call find_psv
0021 |         
0022 |         If Val(comb_find.ListCount) > 0 Then comb_find.DropDown
0023 |         
0024 |         If tb_psv.Text = "" Then
0025 |             If Val(comb_psv.ListCount) > 0 Then
0026 |                 comb_psv.DropDown
0027 |                 Exit Sub
0028 |             End If
0029 |         End If
0030 | 
0031 | End Sub
0032 | 
0033 | 
0034 | Private Sub find_psv()
0035 |     On Error Resume Next
0036 |     
0037 |     str_ = tb_psv.Text
0038 |     
0039 |     If VBA.Len(str_) = 0 Then
0040 |         comb_find.clear
0041 |         comb_find.SetFocus
0042 |         tb_psv.SetFocus
0043 |         Exit Sub
0044 |     End If
0045 |    
0046 |     iCol = 0
0047 |     
0048 |     c = comb_psv.List
0049 |     
0050 |     ReDim cc(LBound(c) To UBound(c), 1 To 1)
0051 |     
0052 |     textS = UCase(str_)
0053 |     
0054 |     For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0055 |         sNm = c(i, 0)
0056 |         
0057 |         If Len(str_) = 1 Then
0058 |             If UCase(VBA.Left(sNm, 1)) = textS Then
0059 |                 cc(i, 1) = c(i, 0)
0060 |                 iCol = iCol + 1
0061 |             End If
0062 |         Else
0063 |             If InStr(1, UCase(sNm), textS) > 0 Then
0064 |                 cc(i, 1) = c(i, 0)
0065 |                 iCol = iCol + 1
0066 |             End If
0067 |         End If
0068 |     Next
0069 |     
0070 |     If iCol = 0 Then
0071 |         comb_find.clear
0072 |         comb_find.SetFocus
0073 |         tb_psv.SetFocus
0074 |         DoEvents
0075 |         Exit Sub
0076 |     End If
0077 | 
0078 |     ReDim w(1 To iCol, 1 To 1)
0079 |     j = 1
0080 |     For i = LBound(cc) To UBound(cc)
0081 |     If cc(i, 1) <> "" Then
0082 |     w(j, 1) = cc(i, 1)
0083 |     j = j + 1
0084 |     End If
0085 |     Next
0086 |     
0087 |     comb_find.clear
0088 |     comb_find.SetFocus
0089 |     tb_psv.SetFocus
0090 |     DoEvents
0091 |     comb_find.List = w
0092 |     
0093 | End Sub
0094 | 
0095 | 
0096 | Private Sub comb_find_Click()
0097 |     On Error Resume Next
0098 |         
0099 |         With comb_find
0100 |             i = .ListIndex
0101 |             If i = -1 Then GoTo 99
0102 |             sZkz = .List(i, 0)
0103 |         End With
0104 |         
0105 |         flag = 1
0106 |         
0107 |         tb_psv.Text = sZkz
0108 |         comb_psv.ListIndex = -1
0109 |         
0110 |         flag = 0
0111 | 99
0112 | End Sub
0113 |

0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub format_pr_()
0005 |         On Error Resume Next
0006 | 
0007 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход")
0008 |         
0009 |             Range(.Cells(row1, prNm), .Cells(row2, prSm)).Borders.LineStyle = True
0010 |             Range(.Cells(row1, prEd), .Cells(row2, prSm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0011 |             Range(.Cells(row1, prCod), .Cells(row2, prCod)).IndentLevel = 1
0012 |

0013 | On Error Resume Next

0015 | r7 = Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0016 | j = 1
0017 | For i = rwZv To r7
0018 | Cells(i, zvNN) = j
0019 | j = j + 1
0020 | Next
0021 | Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm) = Application.Sum(Range(Cells(rwZv, zvSm), Cells(r7 + 4, zvSm)))
0022 | iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(Cells(rwZv, zvNm), Cells(r7 + 3, zvNm)), "<>")
0023 | If iCol = 0 Then Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst) = ""
0024 | End Sub

0040 | Cells(i, prNN) = j
0041 | j = j + 1

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: о_ост_склада ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | 
0002 | 
0003 | Public Sub ost_skds()
0004 |         On Error Resume Next
0005 |         
0006 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0007 |             If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0008 |             
0009 |                     sSk = sk(i, 1)
0010 |                     rw = id(i, 1) + 1
0011 |                     
0012 |                     Call find_cm_sk
0013 |                     Call sk_ost_do
0014 |             
0015 |             End If
0016 |         Next i
0017 | 
0018 | End Sub
0019 | 
0020 | Private Sub sk_ost_do()
0021 |         On Error Resume Next
0022 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("sk_123")
0023 |             If iOperation = "zv" Then .Cells(rw, cm) = .Cells(rw, cm) - CDbl(col(i, 1))
0024 |             If iOperation = "pr" Then .Cells(rw, cm) = .Cells(rw, cm) + CDbl(col(i, 1))
0025 |             If iOperation = "vz" Then .Cells(rw, cm) = .Cells(rw, cm) + CDbl(col(i, 1))
0026 |         End With
0027 | End Sub
0028 | 
0029 | 
0030 | Public Sub find_cm_sk()
0031 |         If sSk = "Материалы" Then cm = 2
0032 |         If sSk = "Металлопрокат" Then cm = 4
0033 |         If sSk = "Спецодежда" Then cm = 6
0034 | End Sub
0035 | 
0036 |

0054 |             .Cells(n7, arhCnZ).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = cnZ

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: ф_корзина ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Dim r As Long: Dim rr As Long
0004 | Dim cell As Range
0005 | 
0006 | 
0007 | Public iCellsOne As String
0008 | Public iCellsTwo As String
0009 | Public iRowBox As Long
0010 | Public sFormula_1 As String
0011 | Public sFormula_2 As String
0012 | 
0013 | 
0014 | 
0015 | 
0016 | Public Sub add_box()
0017 | On Error Resume Next
0018 | iRow = ActiveCell.Row
0019 | Call find_gr
0020 | Call dann
0021 | Call copy_
0022 | If frm_Show.Visible = True Then добавить_контролы
0023 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0024 | r = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0025 | iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r + 3, zvNm)), "<>")
0026 | End With
0027 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0028 | .Cells(3, iBox1) = iCol
0029 | .Cells(3, iBox2) = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина").Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm)
0030 | End With
0031 | End Sub
0032 | 
0033 | 
0034 | Private Sub arr_sk_sk()
0035 | On Error Resume Next
0036 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0037 |     gr_sk = Range(.Cells(5, skGr), .Cells(iRow, skGr)).Value
0038 |     nm_sk = Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(iRow, skNm)).Value
0039 | End With
0040 | End Sub
0041 | 
0042 | Private Sub find_gr()
0043 | On Error Resume Next
0044 | 
0045 | Call arr_sk_sk
0046 | 
0047 | sGr = ""
0048 | 
0049 | For i = UBound(gr_sk) To LBound(gr_sk) Step -1
0050 |     If gr_sk(i, 1) <> "" Then
0051 |     sGr = nm_sk(i, 1)
0052 |     GoTo 99
0053 |     End If
0054 | Next
0055 | 99
0056 | End Sub
0057 | 
0058 | 
0059 | 
0060 | 
0061 | Private Sub dann()
0062 | On Error Resume Next
0063 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0064 | sID = iRow
0065 | sNm = .Cells(iRow, skNm).Value
0066 | sCod = .Cells(iRow, skCod).Value
0067 | sEd = .Cells(iRow, skEd).Value
0068 | sCol = .Cells(iRow, skOst).Value
0069 | sBr = .Cells(iRow, skBr).Value
0070 | sCnZ = .Cells(iRow, skCnZ).Value
0071 | sCnR = .Cells(iRow, skCnR).Value
0072 | sSk = .Cells(iRow, skSk).Value
0073 | End With
0074 | End Sub
0075 | 
0076 | Private Sub copy_()
0077 | On Error Resume Next
0078 | 
0079 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0080 | r = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0081 | If r < rwZv Then r = rwZv: GoTo 22
0082 | For Each cell In Range(.Cells(rwZv, 1), .Cells(r, 1))
0083 | If .Cells(cell.Row, zvSk) = sSk Then
0084 | If CStr(.Cells(cell.Row, zvNm)) = sNm And CStr(.Cells(cell.Row, zvCod)) = sCod Then
0085 | rr = cell.Row
0086 | .Cells(rr, zvCol) = .Cells(rr, zvCol) + 1
0087 | Exit Sub
0088 | End If
0089 | End If
0090 | Next
0091 | 22
0092 | .Cells(r, zvCol).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0093 | .Cells(r, zvCnZ).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0094 | .Cells(r, zvCnR).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0095 | .Cells(r, zvSm).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0096 | .Cells(r, 1) = sID
0097 | .Cells(r, zvSk) = sSk
0098 | .Cells(r, zvNm) = sNm
0099 | .Cells(r, zvCod) = sCod
0100 | .Cells(r, zvEd) = sEd
0101 | .Cells(r, zvCnR) = sCnR
0102 | .Cells(r, zvCnZ) = sCnZ
0103 | .Cells(r, zvOst) = sCol
0104 | .Cells(r, zvBr) = sBr
0105 | .Cells(r, zvCol) = 1
0106 | .Cells(r, zvGr) = sGr
0107 | End With
0108 | 
0109 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0110 |     .Cells(r, zvNN) = r - rwZv + 1
0111 | End With
0112 | 
0113 | iRowBox = r
0114 | Call formula_in_box
0115 | 
0116 | End Sub
0117 | 
0118 | Public Sub del_poz_box()
0119 | On Error Resume Next
0120 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0121 | .Cells(iRow, 2).EntireRow.Delete
0122 | r = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0123 | j = 1
0124 | For i = rwZv To r
0125 | .Cells(i, zvNN) = j
0126 | j = j + 1
0127 | Next
0128 | End With
0129 | End Sub
0130 | 
0131 | 
0132 | Public Sub formula_in_box()
0133 |         On Error Resume Next
0134 |         
0135 |         If iRowBox = 0 Then Exit Sub
0136 |         
0137 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("корзина")
0138 |         
0139 |             iCellsOne = .Cells(iRowBox, zvCol).Address(RowAbsolute:=False, ColumnAbsolute:=False)
0140 |             iCellsTwo = .Cells(iRowBox, zvCnR).Address(RowAbsolute:=False, ColumnAbsolute:=False)
0141 |             sFormula_1 = "=" & iCellsOne & "*" & iCellsTwo
0142 |             .Cells(iRowBox, zvSm).Formula = sFormula_1
0143 |             
0144 |             r24 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 9
0145 |             iCellsOne = .Cells(rwZv, zvSm).Address(RowAbsolute:=False, ColumnAbsolute:=False)
0146 |             iCellsTwo = .Cells(r24, zvSm).Address(RowAbsolute:=False, ColumnAbsolute:=False)
0147 |             sFormula_2 = "=SUM(" & iCellsOne & ":" & iCellsTwo & ")"
0148 |             .Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm).Formula = sFormula_2
0149 |             
0150 |         End With
0151 | 
0152 | End Sub


=== КОМПОНЕНТ: о_ост_обновить_zk ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim cc()
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub ost_sk_zk()
0005 |         On Error Resume Next
0006 |         Call arr_this
0007 |         Call перебрать_sk
0008 |         Call resize_this_ost
0009 | End Sub
0010 | 
0011 | Private Sub arr_this()
0012 |         On Error Resume Next
0013 |         
0014 |         row1 = 5
0015 |         
0016 |         If shNm = "Отложено_расход" Then
0017 |             row2 = ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm).Cells(Rows.Count, zkNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0018 |             Call arr_zk_this
0019 |         End If
0020 |         
0021 |         If shNm = "Отложено_приход" Then
0022 |             row2 = ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm).Cells(Rows.Count, pzkNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0023 |             Call arr_zk_this_pr
0024 |         End If
0025 |         
0026 |         ReDim cc(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To 1)
0027 |         
0028 | End Sub
0029 | 
0030 | Private Sub resize_this_ost()
0031 |         On Error Resume Next
0032 |         
0033 |         If shNm = "Отложено_расход" Then
0034 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm).Cells(5, zkOst).Resize(UBound(cc), 1) = cc
0035 |         End If
0036 |         
0037 |         If shNm = "Отложено_приход" Then
0038 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm).Cells(5, pzkOst).Resize(UBound(cc), 1) = cc
0039 |         End If
0040 | 
0041 | End Sub
0042 | 
0043 | Private Sub перебрать_sk()
0044 |         On Error Resume Next
0045 |         Call load_sk
0046 |         For n = 0 To dic_sk.Count - 1
0047 |         If dic_sk.Item(n) <> "" Then
0048 |         sSk = dic_sk.Item(n): Waite.Label2.Caption = sSk: DoEvents
0049 |         flag = 0
0050 |         Call arr_sk_
0051 |         End If
0052 | 33
0053 |         Next
0054 | End Sub
0055 | 
0056 | Private Sub arr_sk_()
0057 |         On Error Resume Next
0058 |         
0059 |         Call find_cm_sk
0060 |         
0061 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(shNm)
0062 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0063 |             iCol = Application.CountIf(.Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)), "<>")
0064 |             Application.CutCopyMode = False
0065 |         End With
0066 |         
0067 |         If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0068 |         
0069 | Call arr_select_sk
0070 | 
0071 |         Call parse
0072 | 
0073 | End Sub
0074 | 
0075 | 
0076 | Private Sub parse()
0077 |         On Error Resume Next
0078 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0079 |             If sk(i, 1) = sSk Then
0080 |             If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0081 |             
0082 |             For ii = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0083 |                 If c(ii, 4) = nm(i, 1) And CStr(c(ii, 3)) = CStr(cod(i, 1)) Then
0084 |                 cc(i, 1) = c(ii, 6)
0085 |                 GoTo 33
0086 |                 End If
0087 |             Next ii
0088 | 33
0089 |             End If
0090 |             End If
0091 |         Next i
0092 | End Sub
0093 |

0073 |         Range(Cells(rw, pzkNom), Cells(rw, pzkEnd)).Font.Bold = True

0174 | Private Sub diap_this()

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: п_приходовать_zv ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Public Sub prihod_()
0005 | 
0006 |         Call unload_mn_vid_pr: DoEvents
0007 |         
0008 |         With Sheets("Приход")
0009 |         r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, prNm).End(xlUp).Row
0010 |         If r7 < rwZv Then
0011 |         MsgBox "          Нет позиций в накладной!" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0012 |         "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0013 |         "Нажмите кнопку <Добавить позицию> и двойным кликом выберите позиции", 64, "Приход"
0014 |         Exit Sub
0015 |         End If
0016 |         End With
0017 |         
0018 |         sZkz = Cells(rwPr_zkz, 4).Value
0019 |         sDt = VBA.CDate(Cells(rwPr_dt, 4).Value)
0020 |         
0021 |         If MsgBox("     Приходовать накладную?               " & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0022 |         "---------------------------------------------------" & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0023 |         "   Контрагент: " & sZkz & VBA.Chr(10) & _
0024 |         "   Дата:     " & sDt, vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Приход") = vbCancel Then Exit Sub
0025 |         
0026 |         Call doScreenOff
0027 |         Call do_otg
0028 |         Call doScreenOn
0029 | End Sub
0030 | 
0031 | Private Sub do_otg()
0032 | 
0033 |         Call doOst:        Waite.Label2.Caption = "сохранить накладную...": DoEvents
0034 |         Call svPr:         Waite.Label2.Caption = "очистить данные...": DoEvents
0035 | 
0036 |         Call clearBf:      Waite.Label2.Caption = "clear_this...": DoEvents
0037 |         Call clear_this:   Waite.Label2.Caption = "завершение...": DoEvents
0038 | 
0039 |         Call do_sklad_obnovitt:   Waite.Label2.Caption = "обновить_данные...": DoEvents
0040 | 
0041 |         Call erase_arr_zv
0042 |         Call erase_arr_sk
0043 |         
0044 |         Sheets("Приход").Select
0045 | End Sub
0046 | 
0047 | Private Sub dann()
0048 |         On Error Resume Next
0049 |         marker = "c" & VBA.Now
0050 |         Call dann_pr
0051 | End Sub
0052 | 
0053 | 
0054 | 
0055 | Private Sub doOst()
0056 |         iOperation = "pr"
0057 |         Call arr_pr
0058 |         Call ost_skds
0059 | End Sub
0060 |  
0061 |  
0062 | 
0063 | Private Sub svPr()
0064 |         On Error Resume Next
0065 |         iVid = "pr"
0066 |         Call dann
0067 |         Call save_nk
0068 | End Sub
0069 | 
0070 | 
0071 | Private Sub clear_this()
0072 |         On Error Resume Next
0073 | 
0074 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход")
0075 |             If .Cells(9, zvOst) <> "Режим_редактирования" Then
0076 |                 Call nom_nk(3)
0077 |                 .Range("d2") = nomer
0078 |             End If
0079 |         End With
0080 |         
0081 |         Call режим_редактирования_off_pr("Приход")
0082 | 
0083 | 
0084 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход")
0085 |             r7 = .UsedRange.Rows.Count + .UsedRange.Row - 1
0086 |             .Range("a" & rwZv & ":a" & r7 + 44).EntireRow.Delete
0087 |             .Range("a1") = ""
0088 |             .Cells(1, prComm) = ""
0089 | .Cells(9, zvOst) = ""
0090 |         End With
0091 |         
0092 | End Sub

0061 |             
0062 |             .Cells(rwPr_zkz, 4).Value = sZkz
0063 |             .Cells(rwPr_mj, 4).Value = sMj
0064 |             .Cells(rwPr_doc, 4).Value = sOsn
0065 |             .Cells(rwPr_dt, 4).Value = sDt
0066 |             
0067 |             .Cells(rwzvSm, prSm) = summ
0068 |             .Cells(1, prComm) = sComm
0069 |             
0070 |             .Cells(1, prDoc) = sDoc
0071 |             .Cells(1, prDocN) = sDocN
0072 |             .Cells(1, prDocDt) = sDocDt
0073 |             
0074 |         End With
0075 | End Sub
0076 |

0078 |         On Error Resume Next
0079 |

0081 |         
0082 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Отложено_приход")
0083 |         
0084 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkNm), Cells(row2, pzkCnZ)).Copy
0085 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prNm).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0086 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkSm), Cells(row2, pzkSm)).Copy
0087 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prSm).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0088 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkCnR), Cells(row2, pzkCnR)).Copy
0089 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prCnR).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0090 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkNN), Cells(row2, pzkNN)).Copy
0091 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prNN).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0092 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkSk), Cells(row2, pzkSk)).Copy
0093 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prSk).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0094 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkGr), Cells(row2, pzkGr)).Copy
0095 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, prGr).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0096 |             
0097 |             .Range(Cells(row1, pzkID), Cells(row2, pzkID)).Copy
0098 |             ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Приход").Cells(rwZv, 1).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
0099 |             
0100 |             Application.CutCopyMode = False
0101 |

0022 |             If iVid = "ot" Then .Range("g2:k2").EntireColumn.Hidden = flag_hidden

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: frm_print ===
ТИП: UserForm
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | 
0004 | Private Sub OK_Click()
0005 |         On Error Resume Next
0006 |         
0007 |         sPrinter = Me.Label2.Caption
0008 |         iCol_Print = Me.ComboBox1.Value
0009 | 
0010 |         If Me.TextBox1.Text = 1 Then Call prnt_zv
0011 |         If Me.TextBox1.Text = 2 Then Call prnt_pr
0012 |         
0013 | If Me.TextBox1.Text = 3 Then Call prnt_zk
0014 |         If Me.TextBox1.Text = 4 Then Call prnt_zk
0015 |         
0016 |         If Me.TextBox1.Text = 5 Then Call print_ZVK_arh
0017 |         
0018 |         If Me.TextBox1.Text = 7 Then Call prnt_sk
0019 | 
0020 |         Unload Me: DoEvents
0021 | End Sub
0022 | 
0023 | Private Sub prnt_sk()
0024 | On Error Resume Next
0025 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0026 | r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row
0027 | With .PageSetup
0028 | .PrintTitleRows = "$3:$5"
0029 | .PrintArea = "c1:k" & r7
0030 | End With
0031 | .PrintOut Copies:=iCol_Print, ActivePrinter:=sPrinter
0032 | End With
0033 | End Sub
0034 | 
0035 | 
0036 | 
0037 | Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()
0038 | On Error Resume Next
0039 | OK.BackColor = RGB(55, 96, 145)
0040 | OK.ForeColor = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0041 | NO.ForeColor = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0042 | Me.ComboBox1.AddItem "1"
0043 | Me.ComboBox1.AddItem "2"
0044 | Me.ComboBox1.AddItem "3"
0045 | ComboBox1.ListIndex = 0
0046 | Call list_print
0047 | End Sub
0048 | 
0049 | Private Sub list_print()
0050 | On Error Resume Next
0051 | Dim nn
0052 | With CreateObject("Shell.Application").Namespace(4).Items
0053 | For nn = 1 To .Count - 1
0054 | Me.ComboBox2.AddItem .Item(nn).Name
0055 | Next
0056 | End With
0057 | Label2.Caption = Application.ActivePrinter
0058 | Me.ComboBox2.Value = Label2.Caption
0059 | End Sub
0060 | 
0061 | Private Sub ComboBox2_Click()
0062 | On Error Resume Next
0063 | Label2.Caption = ComboBox2.Value
0064 | TextBox1.SetFocus
0065 | End Sub
0066 | 
0067 | Private Sub ComboBox1_Change()
0068 | On Error Resume Next
0069 | OK.SetFocus
0070 | End Sub
0071 | 
0072 | Private Sub NO_Click()
0073 | Unload Me
0074 | End Sub

0040 |             .Cells(shRow, zvCod).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = cod
0041 |             .Cells(shRow, zvEd).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = ed
0042 |             .Cells(shRow, zvCol).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = col
0043 |             .Cells(shRow, zvCnR).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = cnR

0064 |

0066 |

0068 |

0070 |

0072 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvSm), .Cells(r9, zvSm)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0073 |

0075 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0076 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0077 |             End With
0078 | 
0079 |             With Range(.Cells(rwZv, 2), .Cells(r9, zvSm))
0080 |                 .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
0081 |                 .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0082 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0083 |             End With
0084 |

0086 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r9, zvNm)).IndentLevel = 1
0087 | 
0088 |             With Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvNm), .Cells(r9, zvNm))
0089 |                 .WrapText = True
0090 |                 .Rows.AutoFit
0091 |             End With
0092 | 
0093 |             For i = rwZv To r9
0094 |                 .Cells(i, zvNm).RowHeight = .Cells(i, zvNm).RowHeight + 3
0095 |             Next
0096 | 
0097 |         End With

0099 |         Call remove_green

0102 |         ActiveWindow.ScrollColumn = 1
0103 | 
0104 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: склад_обновить ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Public Sub sklad_obnovitt()
0004 |         Call doScreenOff
0005 |         Call do_sklad_obnovitt
0006 |         Call doScreenOn
0007 | End Sub
0008 | 
0009 | Public Sub do_sklad_obnovitt()
0010 |         On Error Resume Next
0011 |         
0012 |         ThisWorkbook.Activate
0013 |         
0014 |         Call arr_sk_this_sheet
0015 |         If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0016 |         
0017 |         Call parse_sk
0018 |         Call do_sklad_show
0019 |         
0020 | End Sub
0021 | 
0022 | Private Sub arr_sk_this_sheet()
0023 |         On Error Resume Next
0024 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0025 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 4
0026 |             nn = Range(.Cells(5, 1), .Cells(r7, 1)).Value
0027 |             nm = Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)).Value
0028 |             iCol = Application.CountIf(Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)), "<>")
0029 |         End With
0030 | End Sub
0031 | 
0032 | Private Sub parse_sk()
0033 |         On Error Resume Next
0034 |         
0035 |         ReDim c(1 To iCol, 1 To 1)
0036 | 
0037 |         j = 1
0038 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0039 |             If nn(i, 1) <> "" Then
0040 |                 c(j, 1) = nm(i, 1)
0041 |                 j = j + 1
0042 |             End If
0043 |         Next
0044 | 
0045 | End Sub
0046 |

0051 |         sMj = Me.comb_Mj.Value
0052 |         sZkz = Me.comb_zkz.Value
0053 |         sCombData = Me.comb_dt.Value
0054 |         
0055 | If (Not Not c) = 0 Then Exit Sub
0056 |         
0057 |         ReDim b(LBound(c) To UBound(c), 1 To iCm)
0058 |         
0059 |         j = 1
0060 |         For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0061 |         
0062 |             If sCombData = "Все" Then GoTo 11
0063 |             If sCombData = "" Then GoTo 11
0064 |             
0065 |             If sCombData = "Сегодня" Then sData = VBA.Format(VBA.Date, "dd.mm.yyyy")
0066 |             If sCombData = "Вчера" Then sData = VBA.Format(VBA.Date - 1, "dd.mm.yyyy")
0067 |             
0068 |             If c(i, 4) = sData Then
0069 | 11
0070 |             If sZkz = "" Then GoTo 22
0071 |             If sZkz = "Все" Then GoTo 22
0072 |             If c(i, 3) = sZkz Then
0073 | 22
0074 |             If sMj = "" Then GoTo 33
0075 |             If sMj = "Все" Then GoTo 33
0076 |             If c(i, 5) = sMj Then
0077 |             
0078 | 33

0080 |                     For cm = 1 To iCm
0081 |                         b(j, cm) = c(i, cm)
0082 |                     Next
0083 |                     j = j + 1
0084 |                 
0085 |             End If
0086 |             End If
0087 |             End If
0088 |             
0089 |         Next
