=== КОМПОНЕНТ: frm_Find ===
ТИП: UserForm
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim w(): Dim cc()
0003 | Dim iCntr As Integer
0004 | 
0005 | Private Sub comb_gr_Change()
0006 | On Error Resume Next
0007 | ind = comb_gr.ListIndex
0008 | If ind = -1 Then Exit Sub
0009 | rw = comb_gr.List(ind, 0) + 4
0010 | Range(Cells(rw, 1), Cells(rw, 33)).Select
0011 | ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = rw - 1
0012 | End Sub
0013 | Private Sub tb_1_Change()
0014 | On Error Resume Next
0015 | Call find_
0016 | If Val(comb_find.ListCount) > 0 Then
0017 | comb_find.DropDown
0018 | End If
0019 | End Sub
0020 | Private Sub tb_2_Change()
0021 | On Error Resume Next
0022 | Call find_
0023 | If Val(comb_find.ListCount) > 0 Then
0024 | comb_find.DropDown
0025 | End If
0026 | End Sub
0027 | Private Sub find_()
0028 | On Error Resume Next
0029 | iCntr = VBA.Right(Me.ActiveControl.Name, 1)
0030 | For n = 1 To 2
0031 | If n <> iCntr Then
0032 | Me.Controls("tb_" & n) = ""
0033 | End If
0034 | Next
0035 | comb_find.clear
0036 | str_ = Me.ActiveControl.Text
0037 | If Len(str_) = 0 Then comb_find.SetFocus: Controls("tb_" & iCntr).SetFocus: Exit Sub
0038 | If str_ = "" Then
0039 | comb_find.SetFocus
0040 | Controls("tb_" & iCntr).SetFocus
0041 | Exit Sub
0042 | End If
0043 | ReDim cc(LBound(c) To UBound(c), 1 To 3)
0044 | iCol = 0
0045 | For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0046 | If Len(str_) = 1 Then
0047 | If VBA.UCase(VBA.Left(c(i, iCntr + 1), 1)) = VBA.UCase(str_) Then
0048 | cc(i, 1) = c(i, 1)
0049 | cc(i, 2) = c(i, 2)
0050 | cc(i, 3) = c(i, 3)
0051 | iCol = iCol + 1
0052 | End If
0053 | Else
0054 | If InStr(1, VBA.UCase(c(i, iCntr + 1)), VBA.UCase(str_)) > 0 Then
0055 | cc(i, 1) = c(i, 1)
0056 | cc(i, 2) = c(i, 2)
0057 | cc(i, 3) = c(i, 3)
0058 | iCol = iCol + 1
0059 | End If
0060 | End If
0061 | Next
0062 | If iCol = 0 Then
0063 | comb_find.clear
0064 | comb_find.SetFocus
0065 | Controls("tb_" & iCntr).SetFocus
0066 | DoEvents
0067 | Exit Sub
0068 | End If
0069 | ReDim w(1 To iCol + 1, 1 To 3)
0070 | j = 1
0071 | For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0072 | If cc(i, 1) <> "" Then
0073 | w(j, 1) = cc(i, 1)
0074 | w(j, 2) = cc(i, 2)
0075 | w(j, 3) = cc(i, 3)
0076 | j = j + 1
0077 | End If
0078 | Next
0079 | comb_find.clear
0080 | comb_find.SetFocus
0081 | Controls("tb_" & iCntr).SetFocus
0082 | DoEvents
0083 | comb_find.List = w
0084 | End Sub

0086 | On Error Resume Next
0087 | ind = comb_find.ListIndex
0088 | If ind = -1 Then Exit Sub
0089 | Me.Caption = "   " & comb_find.List(ind, 1) & "          " & comb_find.List(ind, 2)
0090 | tb_row.Text = comb_find.List(ind, 0)
0091 | rw = Val(tb_row.Value)
0092 | If rw = 0 Then Exit Sub
0093 | Range(Cells(rw, 1), Cells(rw, 33)).Select
0094 | ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = rw - 1

0140 | Private Sub load_sk__()
0141 | On Error Resume Next
0142 | With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Склад")
0143 | r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, skNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0144 | gr = .Range(.Cells(5, skGr), .Cells(r7, skGr)).Value
0145 | cod = .Range(.Cells(5, skCod), .Cells(r7, skCod)).Value
0146 | nm = .Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)).Value
0147 | iCol = Application.CountIf(.Range(.Cells(5, skNm), .Cells(r7, skNm)), "<>")
0148 | End With
0149 | If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0150 | Call parse_arr_sk
0151 | End Sub
0152 | Private Sub parse_arr_sk()
0153 | On Error Resume Next
0154 | ReDim c(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To 3)
0155 | j = 1
0156 | n = 0
0157 | For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0158 | If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0159 | c(j, 1) = i + 4
0160 | c(j, 2) = cod(i, 1)
0161 | c(j, 3) = nm(i, 1)
0162 | If gr(i, 1) <> "" Then
0163 | c(j, 2) = nm(i, 1) & " -----------------------------------------------------------"
0164 | c(j, 3) = "---------------------------------"
0165 | comb_gr.AddItem ""
0166 | comb_gr.List(n, 0) = j
0167 | comb_gr.List(n, 1) = nm(i, 1)
0168 | n = n + 1
0169 | End If
0170 | j = j + 1
0171 | End If
0172 | Next i
0173 | End Sub

0153 | Private Sub Set_Mоnth(MyDate As Date)
0154 | On Error Resume Next
0155 | Dim i As Integer
0156 | Dim j As Integer
0157 | MyYear = VBA.Year(MyDate)
0158 | MyMonth = Month(MyDate)
0159 | MyDay = Day(MyDate)
0160 | Label_Year.Caption = MyYear
0161 | ComboBox_Month.ListIndex = MyMonth - 1
0162 | MyWeekDay = Weekday(DateSerial(MyYear, MyMonth, 1), vbMonday)
0163 | MyCountDay = Day(DateSerial(MyYear, MyMonth + 1, 1) - 1)
0164 | l_start = 2 - MyWeekDay
0165 | For i = 1 To 6
0166 | For j = 1 To 7
0167 | If l_start >= 1 And l_start <= MyCountDay Then
0168 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & i & "_" & j).Caption = l_start
0169 | Else
0170 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & i & "_" & j).Caption = ""
0171 | End If
0172 | If l_start = MyDay Then
0173 | Set_On_Off CInt(i), CInt(j)
0174 | End If
0175 | l_start = l_start + 1
0176 | Next j, i
0177 | End Sub

0180 | dt_1 = VBA.Now
0181 | Set_TextBox_Дата (dt_1)

0185 | mozno = False

0206 | Private Sub Set_Дата(iRow As Integer, jCol As Integer)
0207 | On Error Resume Next
0208 | If Me.Controls("Cell_" & iRow & "_" & jCol).Caption = "" Then Exit Sub
0209 | MyYear = VBA.Year(dt_1)
0210 | MyMonth = Month(dt_1)
0211 | MyDay = CInt(Me.Controls("Cell_" & iRow & "_" & jCol).Caption)

0438 | Dim i As Integer
0439 | Dim j As Integer
0440 | If Me.Controls("Cell_" & iRow & "_" & jCol).Caption = "" Then Exit Sub
0441 | For i = 1 To 6
0442 | For j = 1 To 7
0443 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & i & "_" & j).BackColor = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0444 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & i & "_" & j).BorderColor = RGB(255, 255, 255)
0445 | Next j
0446 | Next i
0447 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & iRow & "_" & jCol).BackColor = RGB(204, 255, 204)
0448 | Me.Controls("Cell_" & iRow & "_" & jCol).BorderColor = RGB(150, 150, 150)
0449 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: печать_apr ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Private Const shRow As Integer = 13
0004 | Private Const cmEnd = 8
0005 | 
0006 | 
0007 | 
0008 | 
0009 | Public Sub prnt_pr()
0010 |         Call doScreenOff
0011 |         Call do_blank
0012 |         Call doScreenOn
0013 | End Sub
0014 | 
0015 | Private Sub do_blank()
0016 |         Call dann_pr
0017 |         Call arr_pr
0018 |         Call copy_to_blank_pr
0019 |         Call print_paper
0020 |         Call clearBlank(shRow)
0021 |         ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank).Visible = 2
0022 | End Sub
0023 | 
0024 | Public Sub copy_to_blank_pr()
0025 |         nmBlank = "prntPr"
0026 |         ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank).Visible = True
0027 |         Call clearBlank(shRow)
0028 |         Call copy_nk
0029 |         Call format_
0030 |         Call copy_dann
0031 |         Call podp_all
0032 |         Call hidden_clm_blank_pr
0033 | End Sub
0034 | 
0035 | Private Sub copy_nk()
0036 |         On Error Resume Next
0037 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank)
0038 |             .Cells(shRow, prNm).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = nm
0039 |             .Cells(shRow, prCod).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = cod
0040 |             .Cells(shRow, prEd).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = ed
0041 |             .Cells(shRow, prCol).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = col
0042 |             .Cells(shRow, prCnZ).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = cnZ
0043 |             .Cells(shRow, prSm).Resize(UBound(nm), 1) = sm
0044 |         End With
0045 | End Sub
0046 | 
0047 | Private Sub copy_dann()
0048 |         On Error Resume Next
0049 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank)
0050 |             .Range("c2").Value = "Приходная накладная № " & nomer & " от " & sDt
0051 |             .Cells(rwPr_zkz, 4).Value = sZkz
0052 |             .Cells(rwPr_mj, 4).Value = sMj
0053 |             .Cells(rwPr_doc, 4).Value = sOsn
0054 |             .Cells(rwPr_dt, 4).Value = sDt
0055 |         End With
0056 | End Sub
0057 | 
0058 | Private Sub format_()
0059 |         On Error Resume Next
0060 | 
0061 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank)
0062 | 
0063 |             r9 = .Cells(Rows.Count, prNm).End(xlUp).Row
0064 |             
0065 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNm), .Cells(r9, prSm)).Borders.LineStyle = True
0066 | 
0067 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prEd), .Cells(r9, prSm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0068 | 
0069 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCnZ), .Cells(r9, prCnZ)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0070 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prSm), .Cells(r9, prSm)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0071 | 
0072 |             With Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNN), .Cells(r9, prNN))
0073 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0074 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0075 |             End With
0076 | 
0077 |             With Range(.Cells(rwZv, 2), .Cells(r9, prSm))
0078 |                 .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
0079 |                 .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0080 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0081 |             End With
0082 | 
0083 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prCod), .Cells(r9, prCod)).IndentLevel = 1
0084 |             Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNm), .Cells(r9, prNm)).IndentLevel = 1
0085 | 
0086 |             With Range(.Cells(rwZv, prNm), .Cells(r9, prNm))
0087 |                 .WrapText = True
0088 |                 .Rows.AutoFit
0089 |             End With
0090 |             
0091 |             j = 1
0092 |             For i = rwZv To r9
0093 |                 .Cells(i, prNm).RowHeight = .Cells(i, prNm).RowHeight + 3
0094 | .Cells(i, prNN) = j
0095 |                 j = j + 1
0096 |             Next
0097 |             
0098 |         End With
0099 | 
0100 |         Call remove_green
0101 |         Range("a1").Select
0102 |         ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = 1
0103 | 
0104 | End Sub
0105 | 
0106 | 
0107 | 
0108 | Private Sub podp_all()
0109 |         Call podp_sm
0110 |         Call podp_podp
0111 | End Sub
0112 | 
0113 | Private Sub podp_sm()
0114 |         On Error Resume Next
0115 |         
0116 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank)
0117 | 
0118 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, prNm).End(xlUp).Row + 1
0119 | 
0120 |             .Cells(r7, prSm).RowHeight = 22
0121 | 
0122 |             .Cells(r7, prCnZ).Value = "Итого:"
0123 | 
0124 |             .Cells(r7, prSm).Value = summ
0125 |             .Cells(r7, prSm).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0126 |             
0127 |             With Range(.Cells(r7, prNN), .Cells(r7, prSm))
0128 |                 .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0129 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0130 |                 .VerticalAlignment = xlCenter
0131 |                 .Font.Bold = True
0132 |                 .Font.Size = 11
0133 |             End With
0134 |             
0135 |         End With
0136 | 
0137 | End Sub
0138 | 
0139 | Private Sub podp_podp()
0140 |         On Error Resume Next
0141 |         r7 = r7 + 2
0142 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("podp")
0143 |             .Rows("3:5").Copy ThisWorkbook.Sheets(nmBlank).Rows(r7)
0144 |             Application.CutCopyMode = False
0145 |         End With
0146 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: я_фигуры ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | 
0002 | Const hh = 2.5
0003 | Const iHeight = 54
0004 | 
0005 | Public Sub shapes_all()
0006 |     Call shapes_height
0007 |     Call shapes_leftt
0008 |     Call shapes_top
0009 | End Sub
0010 | 
0011 | Private Sub shapes_height()
0012 |     With ActiveSheet
0013 |         For i = 1 To 10
0014 |             .Shapes("cmbt_" & i).Height = iHeight
0015 |         Next
0016 |     End With
0017 | End Sub
0018 | 
0019 | 
0020 | Private Sub shapes_leftt()
0021 |     With ActiveSheet
0022 |         .Shapes("cmbt_6").Left = .Shapes("cmbt_1").Left + .Shapes("cmbt_1").Width + hh
0023 |     End With
0024 |     
0025 |     With ActiveSheet.Shapes("cmbt_1")

0308 |         If Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value = "" Then sCol = 0: Exit Sub
0309 |         sCol = Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value
0310 |         If sCol <= 0 Then sCol = 0: Exit Sub
0311 | 33

0313 |         Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value = sCol
0314 | End Sub
0315 | 
0316 | Private Sub SpinButton_SpinUp()
0317 |         On Error Resume Next
0318 |         nom_Cnr = Val(tb_nom.Value)
0319 |         If Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value = "" Then sCol = 0: GoTo 33
0320 |         sCol = Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value
0321 |         If sCol >= Controls("nCol" & nom_Cnr).Value Then sCol = Controls("nCol" & nom_Cnr).Value: Exit Sub
0322 | 33
0323 |         sCol = sCol + 1
0324 |         Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value = sCol
0325 |         If sCol > Controls("nCol" & nom_Cnr).Value Then Controls("nCol_vz" & nom_Cnr).Value = Controls("nCol" & nom_Cnr).Value: Exit Sub
0326 | End Sub

0016 | Public Sub col_Controls()
0017 |         On Error Resume Next
0018 |         iColCtr = 0
0019 |         For Each iCtr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk.Controls
0020 |             If VBA.Left(iCtr.Name, 3) = "nNm" Then
0021 |             iColCtr = iColCtr + 1
0022 |             End If
0023 |         Next
0024 | End Sub
0025 | 
0026 | Public Sub proverka_vz()
0027 | 
0028 |         Call col_Controls
0029 |         
0030 |         iCol = 0
0031 |         
0032 |         With frm_ZVK
0033 |             For i = 1 To iColCtr
0034 |             
0035 |                 str_ = .Controls("nCol_vz" & i).Value
0036 |                 
0037 |                 If .Controls("nCol_vz" & i).Value <> "" Then
0038 |                     If .Controls("nCol_vz" & i).Value <> 0 Then
0039 |                         iCol = iCol + 1
0040 |                     End If
0041 |                 End If
0042 |             Next
0043 |         End With
0044 | 
0045 | End Sub
0046 | 
0047 | 
0048 | Public Sub clear_color_vz()
0049 |         On Error Resume Next
0050 |         
0051 |         For Each iCtr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk.Controls
0052 |             iCtr.BackColor = &H80000005
0053 | 33
0054 |         Next
0055 |         
0056 |         For Each iCtr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk_vz.Controls
0057 |             If iCtr.Name = "comb_sk" Then GoTo 99
0058 |             If iCtr.Name = "SpinButton" Then GoTo 99
0059 |             iCtr.BackColor = &H80000005
0060 | 99
0061 |         Next
0062 |         
0063 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: vz_добавить_контролы ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Private Const hgCntr = 18
0004 | 
0005 | 
0006 | Public Sub добавить_контролы_vz()
0007 | 
0008 |         iColCtr = iCol
0009 |         If iColCtr = 0 Then Exit Sub
0010 |         
0011 |         iVid = zvSelect.comb_vid.Value
0012 | 
0013 |         Call контролы_накладной
0014 |         Call arr_controls_vz
0015 |         Call Frame_height
0016 | 
0017 | End Sub
0018 | 
0019 | Private Sub контролы_накладной()
0020 |         On Error Resume Next
0021 |         
0022 |         iSize = 9
0023 | 
0024 |         ReDim arr_Ctr_zvk(1 To iColCtr)
0025 |         
0026 |         nom_Cnr = 1
0027 |         
0028 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0029 |             If nn(i, 1) <> "" Then
0030 |             
0031 |                 Call dann_poz
0032 |                 Call controls_add
0033 |                 
0034 |                 nom_Cnr = nom_Cnr + 1
0035 |                 
0036 |             End If
0037 |         Next
0038 |         
0039 | End Sub
0040 | 
0041 | Private Sub dann_poz()
0042 |         On Error Resume Next
0043 |         sNN = nn(i, 1)
0044 |         sNm = nm(i, 1)
0045 |         sCod = cod(i, 1)
0046 |         sEd = ed(i, 1)
0047 |         sSm = sm(i, 1)
0048 |         sCol = col(i, 1)
0049 |         sSk = sk(i, 1)
0050 |         
0051 |         If iVid = "Приход" Then sCn = cnZ(i, 1)
0052 |         If iVid = "Отгрузка" Then sCn = cnR(i, 1)
0053 |         If iVid = "Возврат" Then sCn = cnR(i, 1)
0054 |         
0055 | End Sub
0056 | 
0057 | Private Sub arr_controls_vz()
0058 |         On Error Resume Next
0059 | 
0060 |         ReDim arr_Ctr_zvk(1 To nom_Cnr)
0061 | 
0062 | For i = 1 To iColCtr
0063 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nNN = frm_ZVK.Controls("nNN" & i)
0064 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nNm = frm_ZVK.Controls("nNm" & i)
0065 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nCod = frm_ZVK.Controls("nCod" & i)
0066 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nEd = frm_ZVK.Controls("nEd" & i)
0067 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nCn = frm_ZVK.Controls("nCn" & i)
0068 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nSm = frm_ZVK.Controls("nSm" & i)
0069 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nCol = frm_ZVK.Controls("nCol" & i)
0070 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nSk = frm_ZVK.Controls("nSk" & i)
0071 |             
0072 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nCol_vz = frm_ZVK.Controls("nCol_vz" & i)
0073 |             Set arr_Ctr_zvk(i).nSk_vz = frm_ZVK.Controls("nSk_vz" & i)
0074 |             
0075 |         Next

0037 | Private Sub perenos_Height_yes()
0038 |         On Error Resume Next
0039 |         
0040 |         smHeight = 0
0041 |         
0042 |         For i = 1 To iColCtr
0043 |         
0044 |             ReDim c(1 To iCm, 1 To 1)
0045 |             
0046 |             iTop = frm_ZVK.Frame_nk.Controls("nNm" & i).Top
0047 |             Call fimd_max_height
0048 |             
0049 |             iHeightMax = Application.Max(c)
0050 |             If iHeightMax <= hgCntr Then iHeightMax = hgCntr
0051 |             
0052 |             
0053 |             Call высота_в_ряду
0054 |             
0055 | smHeight = smHeight + iHeightMax
0056 |             
0057 |         Next
0058 |         
0059 | End Sub
0060 | 
0061 | Private Sub fimd_max_height()
0062 |         On Error Resume Next
0063 | 
0064 |         j = 1
0065 | 
0066 |         For Each ctr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk.Controls
0067 |             If ctr.Top = iTop Then
0068 |                 iHeight = ctr.Height
0069 |                 c(j, 1) = iHeight
0070 |                 j = j + 1
0071 |             End If
0072 |         Next
0073 |         
0074 | End Sub
0075 | 
0076 | Private Sub высота_в_ряду()
0077 |         On Error Resume Next
0078 | 
0079 |         For Each ctr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk.Controls
0080 |             If ctr.Top = iTop Then
0081 |                 ctr.Height = iHeightMax
0082 |             End If
0083 |         Next
0084 |         
0085 |         For Each ctr In frm_ZVK.Frame_nk_vz.Controls
0086 |             If ctr.Name = "omb_sk" Then GoTo 99
0087 |             If ctr.Name = "SpinButton" Then GoTo 99
0088 |             
0089 |             If ctr.Top = iTop Then
0090 |                 ctr.Height = iHeightMax
0091 |             End If
0092 | 99
0093 |         Next
0094 |         
0095 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: frm_Mnn ===
ТИП: UserForm
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim shName As String
0003 | 
0004 | Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()
0005 |         On Error Resume Next
0006 |         
0007 |         Call forma
0008 |         Call arr_this_sheets
0009 |         Call добавить_контролы_mnn
0010 |         
0011 |         For i = 2 To iCol
0012 |             Controls("nNm" & i).Top = Controls("nNm" & i - 1).Top + Controls("nNm" & i - 1).Height + 1
0013 |         Next
0014 |         
0015 |         iCol = iCol - 1
0016 |         Me.Height = hgCntrMnn * iCol + iCol * iZazor + 32
0017 |         Me.Width = widMnn + 22
0018 |         
0019 | End Sub
0020 | 
0021 | Private Sub forma()
0022 |         On Error Resume Next
0023 |         Me.StartUpPosition = 0
0024 |         With ThisWorkbook.ActiveSheet.Shapes("cmb_mn")
0025 |             Me.Top = .Top + .Height + 15
0026 |             Me.Left = .Left
0027 |         End With
0028 | End Sub
0029 | 
0030 | 
0031 | Private Sub arr_this_sheets()
0032 |         On Error Resume Next
0033 | 
0034 |         Dim sh As Worksheet
0035 |         
0036 |         iCol = 0
0037 |         For Each sh In ThisWorkbook.Sheets
0038 |             If sh.Visible = True Then
0039 |                 iCol = iCol + 1
0040 |             End If
0041 |         Next
0042 |         
0043 |         ReDim nm(1 To iCol, 1 To 1)
0044 |         
0045 |         j = 1
0046 |         For Each sh In ThisWorkbook.Sheets
0047 |             If sh.Visible = True Then
0048 |                 shName = sh.Name
0049 |                 nm(j, 1) = shName
0050 |                 j = j + 1
0051 |             End If
0052 |         Next
0053 | 
0054 | End Sub
0055 | 
0056 | 
0057 | 
0058 | Private Sub UserForm_MouseMove(ByVal Button As Integer, ByVal Shift As Integer, ByVal X As Single, ByVal Y As Single)
0059 |         Call cmb_all
0060 | End Sub
0061 | 
0062 | Private Sub cmb_all()
0063 |         On Error Resume Next
0064 |         For Each ctr In frm_Mnn.Controls
0065 |             ctr.BackColor = frm_Mnn.BackColor
0066 |         Next
0067 | End Sub
0068 |

0004 | Public Const widMnn As Double = 120

0034 |                 nom_Cnr = nom_Cnr + 1
0035 |                 
0036 |             End If
0037 |         Next
0038 |         
0039 | End Sub

0048 |         Next

0064 |             .Name = nmCntr
0065 |             .Caption = sNm
0066 |             
0067 | If sNm = ActiveSheet.Name Then .Height = 0: GoTo 33
0068 |             .Height = hgCntrMnn
0069 |             
0070 | 33
0071 | .Top = 0
0072 |             
0073 |             .BackColor = frm_Mnn.BackColor
0074 |             .BackStyle = 1
0075 |             .Cancel = False
0076 |             .Default = False
0077 |             .TabStop = True
0078 |             
0079 |             .Left = leftCntr
0080 |             .Width = widMnn
0081 |             .Font.Size = 9
0082 |             .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0083 |

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: архив_load ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | Dim sZg As String
0003 | 
0004 | 
0005 | 
0006 | Public Sub load_nk_from_arh()
0007 |         On Error Resume Next
0008 |         
0009 |         Call dann_arh
0010 |         If ind = -1 Then Exit Sub
0011 |         If marker = "" Then Exit Sub
0012 |         
0013 |         Call to_form
0014 |         Call doScreenOn
0015 |

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: frm_Skidka ===

--------------------------------------------------

0002 | Option Explicit

0004 | 
0005 | 
0006 | 
0007 | 
0008 | Private Sub OK_Click()
0009 | 
0010 |         If Me.tb_nm.Value = "" Then Me.tb_nm.Value = 0
0011 | '        If Me.tb_nm.Value = "" Then
0012 | '            MsgBox "Введите процент скидки!!", 64, "Скидка"
0013 | '            tb_nm.SetFocus
0014 | '            DoEvents
0015 | '            Exit Sub
0016 | '        End If
0017 | 
0018 |         Call do_ok
0019 |         
0020 |         Unload Me
0021 | End Sub
0022 | 
0023 | Private Sub do_ok()
0024 |         On Error Resume Next
0025 | 
0026 |         ThisWorkbook.Activate
0027 |         Sheets("Расход").Select
0028 |         
0029 |         iSkid = CDbl(tb_nm.Value)
0030 |         
0031 |         Call arr_zv
0032 | 
0033 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0034 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row + 2
0035 | cn = Range(.Cells(rwZv, zvCn), .Cells(r7, zvCn)).Value
0036 |         End With
0037 |         
0038 |         ReDim cnR(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To 4)
0039 |         ReDim sm(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To 4)
0040 | 
0041 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm)
0042 |             If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0043 |             
0044 |                     sCol = col(i, 1)
0045 |             
0046 |                     sCn = cn(i, 1)
0047 |                     
0048 |                     sCnR = sCn - (sCn * iSkid / 100)
0049 |                     
0050 |                     iSm = sCol * sCnR
0051 |                     
0052 |                     cnR(i, 1) = sCnR
0053 |                     sm(i, 1) = iSm
0054 |                     
0055 |         
0056 |             End If
0057 |         Next
0058 |         
0059 |         
0060 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Расход")
0061 |             .Cells(rwZv, zvCnR).Resize(UBound(sm), 1) = cnR
0062 |             .Cells(rwZv, zvSm).Resize(UBound(sm), 1) = sm
0063 |             
0064 |             .Cells(rwZv_mj, zvOst).Value = iSkid
0065 |         End With
0066 | 
0067 | 
0068 |         r7 = Cells(Rows.Count, zvNm).End(xlUp).Row
0069 |         Cells(rwzvSm, zvSm) = Application.Sum(Range(Cells(rwZv, zvSm), Cells(r7 + 4, zvSm)))
0070 | 
0071 | End Sub
0072 | 
0073 | 
0074 | 
0075 | 
0076 | 
0077 | 
0078 | 
0079 |

0084 |         With ActiveSheet.Shapes("cmb_skidka")
0085 |             Me.Top = .Top + .Height + 20
0086 |             Me.Left = .Left - Me.Width + 20
0087 |         End With
0088 |

0090 |

0235 | Private Sub parse_ost()
0236 | On Error Resume Next
0237 | 
0238 |         Call find_cm_sk
0239 | 
0240 |         With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("sk_123")
0241 |         
0242 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, cm).End(xlUp).Row + 3
0243 |             ost = .Range(.Cells(2, cm), .Cells(r7, cm)).Value
0244 |             
0245 |             For i = LBound(c) To UBound(c)
0246 |             
0247 |                 If c(i, 2) <> "" Then GoTo 22
0248 |                 If IsEmpty(c(i, 2)) Then GoTo 22
0249 |             
0250 |                 If c(i, 2) <> "" Then
0251 |                     c(i, 6) = "---------------------------------"
0252 |                 Else
0253 |                     c(i, 6) = ost(i, 1)
0254 |                 End If
0255 |                 
0256 | 22
0257 |             Next
0258 |             
0259 |         End With
0260 | 
0261 | 
0262 | 
0263 | End Sub

0018 | Private Sub do_filter()
0019 | 
0020 |     On Error Resume Next
0021 | 
0022 |     ReDim sk(1 To 3, 1 To 1)
0023 | 
0024 |     j = 1
0025 | 
0026 |     For i = 0 To ListBox1.ListCount - 1
0027 |         If ListBox1.Selected(i) = True Then
0028 |             sk(j, 1) = ListBox1.List(i, 0)
0029 |             j = j + 1
0030 |         End If
0031 |     Next
0032 | 
0033 |     Call sklad_show
0034 |     
0035 |     Erase c
0036 |     
0037 | End Sub
0038 | 
0039 | Private Sub CheckBox1_Click()
0040 |         On Error Resume Next
0041 | 
0042 |     With ListBox1
0043 |         For i = 0 To .ListCount - 1
0044 |             If CheckBox1.Value = True Then
0045 |                 .Selected(i) = True
0046 |             Else
0047 |                 .Selected(i) = False
0048 |             End If
0049 |         Next
0050 |     End With
0051 | End Sub
0052 | 
0053 | Private Sub check_()
0054 |         On Error Resume Next
0055 | 
0056 |     iCol = 0
0057 |     For i = 0 To ListBox1.ListCount - 1
0058 |         If ListBox1.Selected(i) = True Then
0059 |             iCol = iCol + 1
0060 |         End If
0061 |     Next
0062 | End Sub
0063 | 
0064 | 
0065 | 
0066 | 
0067 | Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()
0068 |         On Error Resume Next
0069 |         
0070 |         Me.StartUpPosition = 0
0071 |         With ActiveSheet.Shapes("cmb_sk")
0072 |         Me.Top = .Top + .Height + 20
0073 |         Me.Left = .Left
0074 |         End With
0075 | 
0076 |         ListBox1.ListStyle = fmListStyleOption
0077 |         ListBox1.MultiSelect = fmMultiSelectMulti
0078 | 
0079 |         Call load_sklads
0080 | End Sub

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: о_otchet_format ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Dim arr_wid()
0004 | Dim sZg As String
0005 | Dim iMin
0006 | Dim iMax
0007 | 
0008 | Private Const vNom As Integer = 2
0009 | Private Const vDt As Integer = 3
0010 | Private Const vNm As Integer = 4
0011 | Private Const vCod As Integer = 5
0012 | Private Const vCol As Integer = 6
0013 | 
0014 | Dim vCn As Integer: Dim vCnZ As Integer: Dim vCnR As Integer
0015 | Dim vSm As Integer: Dim vSmZ As Integer: Dim vSmR As Integer
0016 | Dim vMj As Integer: Dim vZkz As Integer: Dim vDoc As Integer
0017 | Dim vSk As Integer: Dim vOpl As Integer: Dim vSkid As Integer: Dim vPR As Integer
0018 | Dim vEnd As Integer
0019 | 
0020 | 
0021 | Public Sub format_otchet()
0022 |         Call cm_column
0023 |         Call format_otchet_all
0024 |         If iVid = "pr" Then Call format_otchet_pr
0025 |         If iVid = "ot" Then Call format_otchet_ot
0026 | End Sub
0027 | 
0028 | Private Sub cm_column()
0029 | 
0030 |         If iVid = "pr" Then
0031 |             vCn = 7
0032 |             vSm = 8
0033 |             vMj = 9
0034 |             vZkz = 10
0035 |             vDoc = 11
0036 |             vEnd = 11
0037 |         End If
0038 | 
0039 |         If iVid = "ot" Then
0040 |             
0041 |             vCnR = 7
0042 |             vSmR = 8
0043 |             vCnZ = 9
0044 |             vSmZ = 10
0045 |             
0046 |             vPR = 11
0047 |             vMj = 12
0048 |             vZkz = 13
0049 |             vSk = 14
0050 |             vOpl = 15
0051 |             vSkid = 16
0052 |             vEnd = 16
0053 |         End If
0054 | 
0055 | End Sub
0056 | 
0057 | 
0058 | 
0059 | Private Sub format_otchet_ot()
0060 |         Call format_otchet_do_ot
0061 |         Call format_otchet_zg_ot
0062 | End Sub
0063 | 
0064 | Private Sub format_otchet_do_ot()
0065 |         On Error Resume Next
0066 |         
0067 |         With wbOt.ActiveSheet
0068 |         
0069 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, vNm).End(xlUp).Row
0070 |             
0071 |             Range(.Cells(5, vNom), .Cells(r7, vEnd)).Borders.LineStyle = True
0072 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCol), .Cells(r7, vPR)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0073 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCnR), .Cells(r7, vPR)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0074 |             
0075 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCnR), .Cells(r7, vSmR)).Font.ColorIndex = 3
0076 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCnZ), .Cells(r7, vSmZ)).Font.ColorIndex = 10
0077 |             
0078 |             With Range(.Cells(5, vSk), .Cells(r7, vSk))
0079 |                 .Font.Size = 9
0080 |                 .IndentLevel = 1
0081 |             End With
0082 |             
0083 |             With Range(.Cells(5, vOpl), .Cells(r7, vOpl))
0084 |                 .Font.Size = 9
0085 |                 .IndentLevel = 1
0086 |             End With
0087 |             
0088 |             With Range(.Cells(5, vSkid), .Cells(r7, vSkid))
0089 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0090 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0091 |             End With
0092 |             
0093 |         End With
0094 |         
0095 | End Sub
0096 | 
0097 | Private Sub format_otchet_zg_ot()
0098 | 
0099 |         If ThisWorkbook.Sheets("setting").Range("b8").Value = 0 Then GoTo 33
0100 |         With wbOt.ActiveSheet
0101 |             
0102 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, vNm).End(xlUp).Row
0103 |             
0104 |             .Cells(2, vSmR).Formula = "=SUBTOTAL(9,h5:h" & r7 + 1 & ")"
0105 |             
0106 |             .Cells(2, vSmZ).Formula = "=SUBTOTAL(9,j5:j" & r7 + 1 & ")"
0107 |         
0108 |             .Cells(2, vPR).Formula = "=h2-j2"
0109 |             
0110 |             With Range(.Cells(2, "h"), .Cells(2, "k"))
0111 |                 .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0112 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0113 |                 .VerticalAlignment = xlCenter
0114 |                 .HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0115 |                 .Font.Bold = True
0116 |                 .NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0117 |             End With
0118 |         
0119 |         End With
0120 | 33
0121 | 
0122 |         ReDim arr_wid(1 To iCmOt + 1, 2)
0123 |         
0124 |         arr_wid(1, 1) = 1:   arr_wid(1, 2) = ""

0262 |             Range(.Cells(5, vDoc), .Cells(r7, vDoc)).IndentLevel = 1
0263 |             Range(.Cells(5, vDoc), .Cells(r7, vDoc)).Font.Size = 9
0264 |             
0265 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCol), .Cells(r7, vSm)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0266 |             
0267 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCn), .Cells(r7, vSm)).NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"
0268 |             
0269 |         End With
0270 |         
0271 | End Sub
0272 | 
0273 | 
0274 | 
0275 | Private Sub format_otchet_all()
0276 |         On Error Resume Next
0277 |

0279 |     
0280 |         With wbOt.ActiveSheet
0281 |         
0282 |             r7 = .Cells(Rows.Count, vNm).End(xlUp).Row
0283 |             
0284 |             With Range(.Cells(5, vNom), .Cells(r7, vEnd))
0285 |                 .Font.Name = "Times New Roman"
0286 |                 .Font.Size = 10
0287 |                 .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
0288 |             End With
0289 |             
0290 |             Range(.Cells(5, vNm), .Cells(r7, vNm)).IndentLevel = 1
0291 |             Range(.Cells(5, vCod), .Cells(r7, vCod)).IndentLevel = 1
0292 |             Range(.Cells(5, vMj), .Cells(r7, vMj)).IndentLevel = 1
0293 |             Range(.Cells(5, vZkz), .Cells(r7, vZkz)).IndentLevel = 1
0294 |

0296 |             Range(.Cells(5, vMj), .Cells(r7, vMj)).Font.Size = 10
0297 |             
0298 |             Range(.Cells(5, vNom), .Cells(r7, vDt)).HorizontalAlignment = xlCenter
0299 |             Range(.Cells(5, vNom), .Cells(r7, vNom)).NumberFormat = "00000"
0300 |             Range(.Cells(5, vDt), .Cells(r7, vDt)).NumberFormat = "dd.mm.yyyy"
0301 |             
0302 |             Range(.Cells(4, vNom), .Cells(r7, vEnd)).AutoFilter
0303 |         
0304 |         End With
0305 |         
0306 |         ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = 1
0307 |         Call remove_green
0308 |

0310 |

0312 |         
0313 | End Sub

0321 |         End With

0325 |             .Cells(1, 2).EntireRow.Insert
0326 |             .Cells(1, 2).EntireRow.Insert
0327 |             .Cells(1, 2).EntireRow.Insert
0328 |         End With
0329 |

0337 |             iMax = Application.Max(Range(.Cells(5, vDt), .Cells(r7, vDt)))

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: о_otchet ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Public iCmOt As Integer
0002 | Public wbOt As Workbook
0003 | 
0004 | 
0005 | Public Sub otchet_do()

0007 |         Call do_otchet_do
0008 |         Call doScreenOn
0009 | End Sub

0011 | Private Sub do_otchet_do()
0012 | 
0013 |         Call find_vid_arhh
0014 |         Call do_otchet
0015 |         
0016 |         Set wbOt = Nothing
0017 |         Call erase_arr_arh_this
0018 |         Erase c
0019 | End Sub
0020 | 
0021 | Private Sub do_otchet()
0022 |         On Error Resume Next
0023 | 
0024 |         Call arr_arh_for_otchet
0025 |         If iCol = 0 Then Exit Sub
0026 |         
0027 |         Call parse_arh
0028 |         
0029 |         Call resize_arh
0030 |         
0031 |         Call set_otchet
0032 |         
0033 | End Sub
0034 | 
0035 | 
0036 | Private Sub resize_arh()
0037 |         On Error Resume Next
0038 | 
0039 |         Application.Workbooks.Add (1)
0040 |         Set wbOt = ActiveWorkbook
0041 |         
0042 |         With wbOt.ActiveSheet
0043 |             .Cells(2, 2).Resize(UBound(c), iCmOt) = c
0044 |         End With
0045 |         
0046 |         Call format_otchet
0047 |         
0048 | End Sub
0049 | 
0050 | 
0051 | Private Sub parse_arh()
0052 |         If iVid = "pr" Then iCmOt = 10: Call parse_arh_pr
0053 |         If iVid = "ot" Then iCmOt = 15: Call parse_arh_ot
0054 | End Sub
0055 | 
0056 | Private Sub parse_arh_pr()
0057 |         On Error Resume Next
0058 | 
0059 |         ReDim c(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To iCmOt)
0060 |         
0061 |         j = 1
0062 |         
0063 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm): Waite.Label2.Caption = nm(i, 1): DoEvents
0064 |             
0065 |             If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0066 |             
0067 |                     c(j, 1) = nom(i, 1)
0068 |                     c(j, 2) = dt(i, 1)
0069 |                     c(j, 3) = nm(i, 1)
0070 |                     c(j, 4) = cod(i, 1)
0071 |                     c(j, 5) = col(i, 1)
0072 |                     c(j, 6) = cnZ(i, 1)
0073 |                     c(j, 7) = sm(i, 1)
0074 |                     c(j, 8) = mj(i, 1)
0075 |                     c(j, 9) = zkz(i, 1)
0076 |                     c(j, 10) = doc(i, 1)
0077 |                     
0078 |                     j = j + 1
0079 |                 
0080 |             End If
0081 |                 
0082 |         Next i
0083 | 
0084 | End Sub
0085 | 
0086 | Private Sub parse_arh_ot()
0087 |         On Error Resume Next
0088 | 
0089 |         ReDim c(LBound(nm) To UBound(nm), 1 To iCmOt)
0090 |         
0091 |         j = 1
0092 |         
0093 |         For i = LBound(nm) To UBound(nm): Waite.Label2.Caption = nm(i, 1): DoEvents
0094 |             
0095 |             If nm(i, 1) <> "" Then
0096 |             
0097 |                 c(j, 1) = nom(i, 1)
0098 |                 c(j, 2) = dt(i, 1)
0099 |                 c(j, 3) = nm(i, 1)
0100 |                 c(j, 4) = cod(i, 1)
0101 |                 c(j, 5) = col(i, 1)
0102 |                 c(j, 6) = cnR(i, 1)
0103 |                 c(j, 7) = sm(i, 1)
0104 |                 c(j, 8) = cnZ(i, 1)
0105 |                 
0106 |                 сумма_закуп = col(i, 1) * cnZ(i, 1)
0107 |                 c(j, 9) = сумма_закуп
0108 |                 
0109 | c(j, 10) = sm(i, 1) - сумма_закуп
0110 |                 c(j, 11) = mj(i, 1)
0111 |                 c(j, 12) = zkz(i, 1)
0112 |                 
0113 |                 c(j, 13) = sk(i, 1)
0114 |                 c(j, 14) = opl(i, 1)
0115 |                 c(j, 15) = skid(i, 1)
0116 | 
0117 |                 j = j + 1
0118 |                 
0119 |             End If
0120 |                 
0121 |         Next i
0122 | 
0123 | End Sub
0124 | 
0125 |

=== КОМПОНЕНТ: Add_Damp ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | Public Sub ExportVBAProjectToTxt_UTF8()
0004 |     Dim filePath As String
0005 |     Dim comp As Object
0006 |     Dim i As Long
0007 |     Dim stream As Object
0008 |     Dim lineContent As String
0009 |     
0010 |     ' Путь к файлу
0011 |     filePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\VBA_Sklad_Dump_UTF8.txt"
0012 | 
0013 |     ' Создаем объект потока
0014 |     Set stream = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
0015 |     
0016 |     With stream
0017 |         .Type = 2 ' adTypeText
0018 |         .Charset = "utf-8" ' Устанавливаем UTF-8
0019 |         .Open
0020 |         
0021 |         ' Пишем заголовок (добавим кириллицу для проверки кодировки)
0022 |         .WriteText "===== ЭКСПОРТ ПРОЕКТА VBA (UTF-8) =====" & vbCrLf
0023 |         .WriteText "Книга: " & ThisWorkbook.Name & vbCrLf
0024 |         .WriteText "Дата: " & Now & vbCrLf
0025 |         .WriteText String(50, "=") & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
0026 | 
0027 |         ' ==== ДЕРЕВО ПРОЕКТА ====
0028 |         .WriteText "### СТРУКТУРА ПРОЕКТА ###" & vbCrLf
0029 |         For Each comp In ThisWorkbook.VBProject.VBComponents
0030 |             .WriteText "- " & comp.Name & " (" & ComponentTypeName(comp.Type) & ")" & vbCrLf
0031 |         Next comp
0032 |         .WriteText String(50, "-") & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
0033 | 
0034 |         ' ==== КОД МОДУЛЕЙ ====
0035 |         For Each comp In ThisWorkbook.VBProject.VBComponents
0036 |             .WriteText "=== КОМПОНЕНТ: " & comp.Name & " ===" & vbCrLf
0037 |             .WriteText "ТИП: " & ComponentTypeName(comp.Type) & vbCrLf
0038 |             .WriteText String(50, "-") & vbCrLf
0039 | 
0040 |             If comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines > 0 Then
0041 |                 For i = 1 To comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines
0042 |                     ' Читаем строку кода
0043 |                     lineContent = comp.CodeModule.Lines(i, 1)
0044 |                     ' Записываем с номером строки
0045 |                     .WriteText Format(i, "0000") & " | " & lineContent & vbCrLf
0046 |                 Next i
0047 |             Else
0048 |                 .WriteText "[Пустой модуль]" & vbCrLf
0049 |             End If
0050 | 
0051 |             .WriteText vbCrLf & vbCrLf
0052 |         Next comp
0053 | 
0054 |         ' Сохраняем (2 = перезаписать файл)
0055 |         .SaveToFile filePath, 2
0056 |         .Close
0057 |     End With
0058 | 
0059 |     MsgBox "Готово! Файл сохранен в UTF-8:" & vbCrLf & filePath, vbInformation
0060 | End Sub
0061 | 
0062 | Private Function ComponentTypeName(ByVal t As Long) As String
0063 |     Select Case t
0064 |         Case 1: ComponentTypeName = "Standard Module"
0065 |         Case 2: ComponentTypeName = "Class Module"
0066 |         Case 3: ComponentTypeName = "UserForm"
0067 |         Case 100: ComponentTypeName = "ThisWorkbook / Sheet"
0068 |         Case Else: ComponentTypeName = "Unknown"
0069 |     End Select
0070 | End Function


=== КОМПОНЕНТ: ExportANCI ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | ' ================================================================
0004 | ' МОДУЛЬ: modGitExport
0005 | ' Экспорт VBA-компонентов в папку srcCloude/ для GitHub/Claude
0006 | ' ================================================================
0007 | ' Структура:
0008 | '   src/
0009 | '     modules/    — стандартные модули (.bas)
0010 | '     classes/    — классы (.cls)
0011 | '     forms/      — формы (.frm)
0012 | '     sheets/     — код листов и ЭтойКниги (.bas, cp1251)
0013 | '
0014 | ' .gitignore: *.frx
0015 | ' ================================================================
0016 | 
0017 | Private Const EXPORT_ROOT As String = "srcCloudeANCI"
0018 | 
0019 | Private Type ExportResult
0020 |     Exported As Long
0021 |     Skipped  As Long
0022 |     Errors   As Long
0023 |     ErrorLog As String
0024 | End Type
0025 | 
0026 | 
0027 | ' ================================================================
0028 | ' ТОЧКА ВХОДА
0029 | ' ================================================================
0030 | Public Sub ExportAllModulesANCI()
0031 | 
0032 |     Dim result   As ExportResult
0033 |     Dim rootPath As String
0034 | 
0035 |     rootPath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\" & EXPORT_ROOT & "\"
0036 | 
0037 |     EnsureFolder rootPath
0038 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "modules\"
0039 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "classes\"
0040 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "forms\"
0041 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "sheets\"
0042 | 
0043 |     Dim comp As Object
0044 |     For Each comp In ThisWorkbook.VBProject.VBComponents
0045 |         ExportComponent comp, rootPath, result
0046 |     Next comp
0047 | 
0048 |     Dim msg As String
0049 |     msg = "Экспорт завершён:" & vbCrLf & _
0050 |           "  Экспортировано: " & result.Exported & vbCrLf & _
0051 |           "  Пропущено:      " & result.Skipped
0052 | 
0053 |     If result.Errors > 0 Then
0054 |         msg = msg & vbCrLf & "  Ошибок: " & result.Errors & _
0055 |               vbCrLf & vbCrLf & result.ErrorLog
0056 |         MsgBox msg, vbExclamation, "Экспорт VBA"
0057 |     Else
0058 |         MsgBox msg & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & rootPath, vbInformation, "Экспорт VBA"
0059 |     End If
0060 | 
0061 | End Sub
0062 | 
0063 | 
0064 | ' ================================================================
0065 | ' МАРШРУТИЗАЦИЯ КОМПОНЕНТА
0066 | ' ================================================================
0067 | Private Sub ExportComponent( _
0068 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0069 |     ByVal rootPath As String, _
0070 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0071 | )
0072 |     ' Сам себя не экспортируем
0073 |     If comp.Name = "modGitExport" Or comp.Name = "ADD_VBA_Dump" Then
0074 |         result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0075 |         Exit Sub
0076 |     End If
0077 | 
0078 |     Select Case comp.Type
0079 | 
0080 |         Case 1   ' StdModule
0081 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "modules\" & comp.Name & ".bas", result
0082 | 
0083 |         Case 2   ' ClassModule
0084 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "classes\" & comp.Name & ".cls", result
0085 | 
0086 |         Case 3   ' MSForm
0087 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "forms\" & comp.Name & ".frm", result
0088 | 
0089 |         Case 100 ' Document (листы, ЭтаКнига)
0090 |             ExportDocumentModule comp, rootPath & "sheets\", result
0091 | 
0092 |         Case Else
0093 |             result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0094 | 
0095 |     End Select
0096 | End Sub
0097 | 
0098 | 
0099 | ' ================================================================
0100 | ' ЭКСПОРТ ЧЕРЕЗ comp.Export (модули, классы, формы)
0101 | ' ================================================================
0102 | Private Sub ExportViaAPI( _
0103 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0104 |     ByVal filePath As String, _
0105 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0106 | )
0107 |     On Error GoTo Fail
0108 |     comp.Export filePath
0109 |     result.Exported = result.Exported + 1
0110 |     Exit Sub
0111 | Fail:
0112 |     result.Errors = result.Errors + 1
0113 |     result.ErrorLog = result.ErrorLog & comp.Name & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf
0114 |     On Error GoTo 0
0115 | End Sub
0116 | 
0117 | 
0118 | ' ================================================================
0119 | ' ЭКСПОРТ КОДА ЛИСТА / ЭТОЙКНИГИ ЧЕРЕЗ ADODB.Stream (cp1251)
0120 | '
0121 | ' Почему нельзя comp.Export:
0122 | '   Document-компоненты привязаны к объекту книги, Excel
0123 | '   не позволяет экспортировать их как отдельный файл —
0124 | '   метод Export для Type=100 выбрасывает ошибку.
0125 | '
0126 | ' Почему cp1251, а не UTF-8:
0127 | '   VBA при импорте .bas/.cls читает файлы в системной кодировке
0128 | '   (cp1251 для русских Windows). UTF-8 без BOM приведёт к
0129 | '   кракозябрам в строковых константах при повторном импорте.
0130 | '   Для просмотра на GitHub/Claude кодировка не важна —
0131 | '   GitHub автоопределяет её.
0132 | ' ================================================================
0133 | Private Sub ExportDocumentModule( _
0134 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0135 |     ByVal folderPath As String, _
0136 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0137 | )
0138 |     ' Пропускаем компоненты без кода
0139 |     If comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines = 0 Then
0140 |         result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0141 |         Exit Sub
0142 |     End If
0143 | 
0144 |     ' Читаем строки через CodeModule — единственный надёжный способ
0145 |     ' получить код Document-компонента программно
0146 |     Dim i       As Long
0147 |     Dim content As String
0148 | 
0149 |     ' Заголовок-комментарий: имя компонента и тип объекта
0150 |     Dim objName As String
0151 |     On Error Resume Next
0152 |     ' Для листов — имя вкладки; для ThisWorkbook — имя файла
0153 |     objName = comp.Properties("Name").Value
0154 |     On Error GoTo 0
0155 |     If objName = "" Then objName = comp.Name
0156 | 
0157 |     content = "' Component: " & comp.Name & "  [" & objName & "]" & vbCrLf & _
0158 |               "' Type: Document (Sheet / ThisWorkbook)" & vbCrLf & _
0159 |               "Option Explicit" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
0160 | 
0161 |     ' Пропускаем первую строку если это уже "Option Explicit"
0162 |     ' (CodeModule иногда добавляет её автоматически)
0163 |     Dim startLine As Long
0164 |     startLine = 1
0165 |     If LCase(Trim(comp.CodeModule.Lines(1, 1))) = "option explicit" Then
0166 |         startLine = 2
0167 |     End If
0168 | 
0169 |     For i = startLine To comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines
0170 |         content = content & comp.CodeModule.Lines(i, 1) & vbCrLf
0171 |     Next i
0172 | 
0173 |     ' Имя файла: имя компонента + "_" + имя вкладки (если отличается)
0174 |     Dim fileName As String
0175 |     If objName <> comp.Name And objName <> "" Then
0176 |         fileName = comp.Name & "_" & CleanFileName(objName) & ".bas"
0177 |     Else
0178 |         fileName = comp.Name & ".bas"
0179 |     End If
0180 | 
0181 |     Dim filePath As String
0182 |     filePath = folderPath & fileName
0183 | 
0184 |     ' Запись через ADODB.Stream в cp1251
0185 |     On Error GoTo Fail
0186 |     WriteFileCp1251 filePath, content
0187 |     On Error GoTo 0
0188 | 
0189 |     result.Exported = result.Exported + 1
0190 |     Exit Sub
0191 | 
0192 | Fail:
0193 |     result.Errors = result.Errors + 1
0194 |     result.ErrorLog = result.ErrorLog & comp.Name & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf
0195 |     On Error GoTo 0
0196 | End Sub
0197 | 
0198 | 
0199 | ' ================================================================
0200 | ' ЗАПИСЬ ТЕКСТА В ФАЙЛ В КОДИРОВКЕ cp1251
0201 | ' ================================================================
0202 | Private Sub WriteFileCp1251(ByVal filePath As String, ByVal content As String)
0203 | 
0204 |     Dim stream As Object
0205 |     Set stream = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
0206 | 
0207 |     With stream
0208 |         .Type = 2          ' adTypeText
0209 |         .Charset = "windows-1251"
0210 |         .Open
0211 |         .WriteText content
0212 |         .SaveToFile filePath, 2    ' adSaveCreateOverWrite
0213 |         .Close
0214 |     End With
0215 | 
0216 |     Set stream = Nothing
0217 | End Sub
0218 | 
0219 | 
0220 | ' ================================================================
0221 | ' ОЧИСТКА ИМЕНИ ФАЙЛА ОТ НЕДОПУСТИМЫХ СИМВОЛОВ
0222 | ' ================================================================
0223 | Private Function CleanFileName(ByVal s As String) As String
0224 |     Dim bad As Variant
0225 |     Dim i   As Long
0226 |     bad = Array("\", "/", ":", "*", "?", """", "<", ">", "|", " ")
0227 |     For i = LBound(bad) To UBound(bad)
0228 |         s = Replace(s, bad(i), "_")
0229 |     Next i
0230 |     CleanFileName = s
0231 | End Function
0232 | 
0233 | 
0234 | ' ================================================================
0235 | ' СОЗДАТЬ ПАПКУ (если не существует)
0236 | ' ================================================================
0237 | Private Sub EnsureFolder(ByVal Path As String)
0238 |     If Dir(Path, vbDirectory) = "" Then
0239 |         On Error Resume Next
0240 |         MkDir Path
0241 |         On Error GoTo 0
0242 |     End If
0243 | End Sub
0244 | 
0245 | 
0246 | 


=== КОМПОНЕНТ: ExportUTF8 ===
ТИП: Standard Module
--------------------------------------------------
0001 | Option Explicit
0002 | 
0003 | ' ================================================================
0004 | ' МОДУЛЬ: modGitExport
0005 | ' Экспорт VBA-компонентов в UTF-8 (с BOM) для GitHub
0006 | ' ================================================================
0007 | 
0008 | Private Const EXPORT_ROOT As String = "srcCloudeUTF8"
0009 | 
0010 | Private Type ExportResult
0011 |     Exported As Long
0012 |     Skipped  As Long
0013 |     Errors   As Long
0014 |     ErrorLog As String
0015 | End Type
0016 | 
0017 | 
0018 | ' ================================================================
0019 | ' ТОЧКА ВХОДА
0020 | ' ================================================================
0021 | Public Sub ExportAllModulesUTF8()
0022 | 
0023 |     Dim result   As ExportResult
0024 |     Dim rootPath As String
0025 | 
0026 |     rootPath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\" & EXPORT_ROOT & "\"
0027 | 
0028 |     EnsureFolder rootPath
0029 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "modules\"
0030 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "classes\"
0031 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "forms\"
0032 |     EnsureFolder rootPath & "sheets\"
0033 | 
0034 |     Dim comp As Object
0035 |     For Each comp In ThisWorkbook.VBProject.VBComponents
0036 |         ExportComponent comp, rootPath, result
0037 |     Next comp
0038 | 
0039 |     Dim msg As String
0040 |     msg = "Экспорт завершён:" & vbCrLf & _
0041 |           "  Экспортировано: " & result.Exported & vbCrLf & _
0042 |           "  Пропущено:      " & result.Skipped
0043 | 
0044 |     If result.Errors > 0 Then
0045 |         msg = msg & vbCrLf & "  Ошибок: " & result.Errors & _
0046 |               vbCrLf & vbCrLf & result.ErrorLog
0047 |         MsgBox msg, vbExclamation, "Экспорт VBA"
0048 |     Else
0049 |         MsgBox msg & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & rootPath, vbInformation, "Экспорт VBA"
0050 |     End If
0051 | 
0052 | End Sub
0053 | 
0054 | 
0055 | ' ================================================================
0056 | ' МАРШРУТИЗАЦИЯ
0057 | ' ================================================================
0058 | Private Sub ExportComponent( _
0059 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0060 |     ByVal rootPath As String, _
0061 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0062 | )
0063 |     If comp.Name = "modGitExport" Or comp.Name = "ADD_VBA_Dump" Then
0064 |         result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0065 |         Exit Sub
0066 |     End If
0067 | 
0068 |     Select Case comp.Type
0069 | 
0070 |         Case 1   ' StdModule
0071 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "modules\" & comp.Name & ".bas", result
0072 | 
0073 |         Case 2   ' ClassModule
0074 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "classes\" & comp.Name & ".cls", result
0075 | 
0076 |         Case 3   ' MSForm
0077 |             ExportViaAPI comp, rootPath & "forms\" & comp.Name & ".frm", result
0078 | 
0079 |         Case 100 ' Document
0080 |             ExportDocumentModule comp, rootPath & "sheets\", result
0081 | 
0082 |         Case Else
0083 |             result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0084 | 
0085 |     End Select
0086 | End Sub
0087 | 
0088 | 
0089 | ' ================================================================
0090 | ' ЭКСПОРТ С ПЕРЕКОДИРОВКОЙ ANSI > UTF-8
0091 | ' ================================================================
0092 | Private Sub ExportViaAPI( _
0093 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0094 |     ByVal filePath As String, _
0095 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0096 | )
0097 |     On Error GoTo Fail
0098 | 
0099 |     Dim tempPath As String
0100 |     tempPath = filePath & ".tmp"
0101 | 
0102 |     ' 1. Экспорт в ANSI
0103 |     comp.Export tempPath
0104 | 
0105 |     ' 2. Чтение ANSI
0106 |     Dim content As String
0107 |     content = ReadFileAnsi(tempPath)
0108 | 
0109 |     ' 3. Запись UTF-8 BOM
0110 |     WriteFileUtf8Bom filePath, content
0111 | 
0112 |     ' 4. Удаление временного файла
0113 |     Kill tempPath
0114 | 
0115 |     result.Exported = result.Exported + 1
0116 |     Exit Sub
0117 | 
0118 | Fail:
0119 |     result.Errors = result.Errors + 1
0120 |     result.ErrorLog = result.ErrorLog & comp.Name & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf
0121 |     On Error GoTo 0
0122 | End Sub
0123 | 
0124 | 
0125 | ' ================================================================
0126 | ' ЭКСПОРТ ЛИСТОВ / THISWORKBOOK
0127 | ' ================================================================
0128 | Private Sub ExportDocumentModule( _
0129 |     ByVal comp As Object, _
0130 |     ByVal folderPath As String, _
0131 |     ByRef result As ExportResult _
0132 | )
0133 |     If comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines = 0 Then
0134 |         result.Skipped = result.Skipped + 1
0135 |         Exit Sub
0136 |     End If
0137 | 
0138 |     Dim i       As Long
0139 |     Dim content As String
0140 | 
0141 |     Dim objName As String
0142 |     On Error Resume Next
0143 |     objName = comp.Properties("Name").Value
0144 |     On Error GoTo 0
0145 |     If objName = "" Then objName = comp.Name
0146 | 
0147 |     content = "' Component: " & comp.Name & "  [" & objName & "]" & vbCrLf & _
0148 |               "' Type: Document" & vbCrLf & _
0149 |               "Option Explicit" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
0150 | 
0151 |     Dim startLine As Long
0152 |     startLine = 1
0153 |     If LCase(Trim(comp.CodeModule.Lines(1, 1))) = "option explicit" Then
0154 |         startLine = 2
0155 |     End If
0156 | 
0157 |     For i = startLine To comp.CodeModule.CountOfLines
0158 |         content = content & comp.CodeModule.Lines(i, 1) & vbCrLf
0159 |     Next i
0160 | 
0161 |     Dim fileName As String
0162 |     If objName <> comp.Name And objName <> "" Then
0163 |         fileName = comp.Name & "_" & CleanFileName(objName) & ".bas"
0164 |     Else
0165 |         fileName = comp.Name & ".bas"
0166 |     End If
0167 | 
0168 |     Dim filePath As String
0169 |     filePath = folderPath & fileName
0170 | 
0171 |     On Error GoTo Fail
0172 |     WriteFileUtf8Bom filePath, content
0173 |     On Error GoTo 0
0174 | 
0175 |     result.Exported = result.Exported + 1
0176 |     Exit Sub
0177 | 
0178 | Fail:
0179 |     result.Errors = result.Errors + 1
0180 |     result.ErrorLog = result.ErrorLog & comp.Name & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf
0181 |     On Error GoTo 0
0182 | End Sub
0183 | 
0184 | 
0185 | ' ================================================================
0186 | ' ЧТЕНИЕ ANSI (cp1251)
0187 | ' ================================================================
0188 | Private Function ReadFileAnsi(ByVal filePath As String) As String
0189 | 
0190 |     Dim stm As Object
0191 |     Set stm = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
0192 | 
0193 |     stm.Type = 2
0194 |     stm.Charset = "windows-1251"
0195 |     stm.Open
0196 |     stm.LoadFromFile filePath
0197 | 
0198 |     ReadFileAnsi = stm.ReadText
0199 | 
0200 |     stm.Close
0201 |     Set stm = Nothing
0202 | 
0203 | End Function
0204 | 
0205 | 
0206 | ' ================================================================
0207 | ' ЗАПИСЬ UTF-8 С BOM
0208 | ' ================================================================
0209 | Private Sub WriteFileUtf8Bom(ByVal filePath As String, ByVal content As String)
0210 | 
0211 |     Dim tsText As Object
0212 |     Set tsText = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
0213 | 
0214 |     tsText.Type = 2
0215 |     tsText.Charset = "utf-8"
0216 |     tsText.Open
0217 |     tsText.WriteText content
0218 | 
0219 |     Dim tsBin As Object
0220 |     Set tsBin = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
0221 | 
0222 |     tsBin.Type = 1
0223 |     tsBin.Open
0224 | 
0225 |     tsText.Position = 0
0226 |     tsText.CopyTo tsBin
0227 | 
0228 |     tsBin.SaveToFile filePath, 2
0229 | 
0230 |     tsText.Close
0231 |     tsBin.Close
0232 | 
0233 |     Set tsText = Nothing
0234 |     Set tsBin = Nothing
0235 | 
0236 | End Sub
0237 | 
0238 | 
0239 | ' ================================================================
0240 | ' ОЧИСТКА ИМЕНИ ФАЙЛА
0241 | ' ================================================================
0242 | Private Function CleanFileName(ByVal s As String) As String
0243 |     Dim bad As Variant
0244 |     Dim i   As Long
0245 | 
0246 |     bad = Array("\", "/", ":", "*", "?", """", "<", ">", "|", " ")
0247 | 
0248 |     For i = LBound(bad) To UBound(bad)
0249 |         s = Replace(s, bad(i), "_")
0250 |     Next i
0251 | 
0252 |     CleanFileName = s
0253 | End Function
0254 | 
0255 | 
0256 | ' ================================================================
0257 | ' СОЗДАНИЕ ПАПКИ
0258 | ' ================================================================
0259 | Private Sub EnsureFolder(ByVal Path As String)
0260 |     If Dir(Path, vbDirectory) = "" Then
0261 |         On Error Resume Next
0262 |         MkDir Path
0263 |         On Error GoTo 0
0264 |     End If
0265 | End Sub
0266 |
